-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.drag
local function C_3()
	local script = G2L["3"];
	local gui = script.Parent -- the GUI you want to drag
	local dragging = false
	local dragStart = nil
	local startPos = nil

	-- When the player clicks the GUI
	gui.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = gui.Position

			-- Capture input so we can track when the mouse moves outside GUI
			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
					dragging = false
				end
			end)
		end
	end)

	-- When the player moves the mouse
	gui.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement and dragging then
			local delta = input.Position - dragStart
			gui.Position = UDim2.new(
				startPos.X.Scale,
				startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
				startPos.Y.Scale,
				startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
			)
		end
	end)

end;
task.spawn(C_3);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.LocalScript
local function C_4()
	local script = G2L["4"];
	local UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
	local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

	--// find ALL BindButtons inside script.Parent's descendants
	local BindButtons = {}

	for _, descendant in ipairs(script.Parent:GetDescendants()) do
		if descendant.Name == "BindButton" then
			table.insert(BindButtons, descendant)
		end
	end

	if #BindButtons == 0 then
		warn("No BindButtons found inside script.Parent")
		return
	end

	--// executor file support check
	local canSave = (writefile and readfile and isfile and delfile) ~= nil

	--// setup each button independently
	for i, btn in ipairs(BindButtons) do
		local FILE_NAME = "keybind_" .. i .. ".json"
		local listening = false
		local currentBind = nil

		--// load saved bind for this button
		if canSave and isfile(FILE_NAME) then
			local success, data = pcall(readfile, FILE_NAME)
			if success and data then
				local decoded = HttpService:JSONDecode(data)
				if decoded and decoded.key then
					currentBind = decoded.key
					btn.Text = decoded.key
				end
			end
		end

		--// save bind
		local function saveBind(key)
			if not canSave then return end
			pcall(function()
				writefile(FILE_NAME, HttpService:JSONEncode({ key = key }))
			end)
		end

		--// delete bind file
		local function deleteBind()
			if not canSave then return end
			if isfile(FILE_NAME) then
				pcall(function()
					delfile(FILE_NAME)
				end)
			end
		end

		--// click to start binding
		btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			listening = true

			StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "Keybind",
				Text = "Press any key (Ctrl to Unbind)",
				Duration = 3
			})
		end)

		--// listen for key
		UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
			if gameProcessed then return end
			if not listening then return end

			listening = false

			-- ctrl = unbind
			if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl or input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.RightControl then
				currentBind = nil
				btn.Text = "..."
				deleteBind()
				return
			end

			local keyName = input.KeyCode.Name
			currentBind = keyName
			btn.Text = keyName

			saveBind(keyName)
		end)
	end
end;
task.spawn(C_4);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.borderStrke.borderGrandient.swift
local function C_7()
	local script = G2L["7"];
	local uiGradient = script.Parent
	local tweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

	local gradientTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
		2,
		Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
		Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
		-1,
		false,
		0
	)

	tweenService:Create(uiGradient, gradientTweenInfo, {Rotation = 360}):Play()
end;
task.spawn(C_7);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.ScrollingFrame.Frame.LocalScript
local function C_b()
	local script = G2L["b"];
	local FrameParents = script.Parent.Parent.Parent
	script.Parent["2"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		FrameParents.LaunchFrame.Visible = true
		FrameParents.EspFrame.Visible = false
		FrameParents.FeaturesFrame.Visible = false
	end)
	script.Parent["3"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		FrameParents.FeaturesFrame.Visible = true
		FrameParents.LaunchFrame.Visible = false
		FrameParents.EspFrame.Visible = false
	end)
	script.Parent["4"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		FrameParents.EspFrame.Visible = true
		FrameParents.LaunchFrame.Visible = false
		FrameParents.FeaturesFrame.Visible = false
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_b);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.8.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_22()
	local script = G2L["22"];
	-- AUTO DESTROY TURRET (Sentry Destroyer)
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Finds and destroys enemy sentries every second

	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
	local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false
	local destroyLoop = nil

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	local function destroyAllSentries()
		for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if player ~= LocalPlayer then
				local sentryName = "Sentry_" .. tostring(player.UserId)

				-- Destroy from Workspace
				local sentryWS = Workspace:FindFirstChild(sentryName)
				if sentryWS then sentryWS:Destroy() end

				-- Destroy from ReplicatedStorage templates
				local sentryRS = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild(sentryName)
				if sentryRS then sentryRS:Destroy() end
			end
		end

		-- Also destroy any generic turret models by name patterns
		for _, obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
			if obj:IsA("Model") then
				local name = obj.Name:lower()
				if name:find("sentry") or name:find("turret") then
					-- Only destroy if it doesn't belong to us
					local ownerValue = obj:FindFirstChild("Owner") or obj:FindFirstChild("OwnerId")
					if ownerValue then
						local ownerName = tostring(ownerValue.Value)
						if ownerName ~= LocalPlayer.Name and ownerName ~= tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId) then
							obj:Destroy()
						end
					else
						-- No owner tag — safe to destroy if not ours by sentry naming convention
						if not obj.Name:find(tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId)) then
							obj:Destroy()
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end

	local function startLoop()
		if destroyLoop then return end
		destroyLoop = task.spawn(function()
			while isEnabled do
				destroyAllSentries()
				task.wait(1)
			end
		end)
	end

	local function stopLoop()
		isEnabled = false
		destroyLoop = nil
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			startLoop()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			stopLoop()
		end
	end

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_22);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.7.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_33()
	local script = G2L["33"];
	-- SEMI-INVISIBILITY
	-- script.Parent = TextButton (child Frame for slider indicator)

	--[[
		DEPTH ADDITIONS over original:
		• Config block at the top — all tunable values in one place
		• R6 / R15 rig auto-detection with rig-specific joint rewire logic
		• Animation fallback chain — cycles backup IDs if primary fails to load
		• Health watcher — Heartbeat loop that checks clone/root integrity every
		  N seconds and silently reapplies the exploit if server undoes it
		• Dynamic tool-weld re-wiring — DescendantAdded listener patches Motor6D
		  joints inside newly equipped tools so they don't detach mid-invis
		• Network ownership claiming via sethiddenproperty / SetNetworkOwner
		  so the client has physics authority over the hidden root
		• Hitbox strategy: SINK mode (original) or REMOTE mode (bury root 5000
		  studs underground so server raycasts can't reach it)
		• Per-frame sink jitter — randomised offset stops static-position detection
	]]

	-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
	-- CONFIG
	-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
	local Config = {
		-- Animation IDs tried in order; first successful load wins.
		AnimationIds = {
			"rbxassetid://18537363391",
			"rbxassetid://13800924076",
			"rbxassetid://507766388",
		},

		-- "SINK"   = position hidden root just below the clone (original)
		-- "REMOTE" = bury it 5000 studs underground (no hitbox whatsoever)
		HitboxStrategy = "SINK",

		-- Base vertical offset for SINK mode
		SinkOffset = 0.09,

		-- Per-frame random jitter on SinkOffset (range: +-Jitter)
		SinkJitter = 0.04,

		-- Seconds between integrity checks (health watcher)
		WatcherInterval = 3,

		-- Seconds before another toggle is accepted
		ToggleCooldown = 0.6,
	}

	-- ── Services ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local Players          = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService       = game:GetService("RunService")
	local TweenService     = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local Workspace        = game:GetService("Workspace")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local Camera      = Workspace.CurrentCamera
	local button      = script.Parent
	local sliderFrame = button:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Frame")
	local bindButton  = button.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")

	-- ── State ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local isInvisible    = false
	local isToggling     = false
	local godmodeApplied = false

	local clone, oldRoot, hip, animTrack
	local rigType = "R15"

	-- ── Maid ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local Maid = {}
	function Maid:Add(key, item)
		if not self[key] then self[key] = {} end
		table.insert(self[key], item)
		return item
	end
	function Maid:Clean(key)
		local bucket = self[key]
		if not bucket then return end
		for _, item in ipairs(bucket) do
			if typeof(item) == "RBXScriptConnection" then item:Disconnect()
			elseif type(item) == "function" then pcall(item) end
		end
		self[key] = {}
	end

	-- ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function Tween(obj, t, style, dir, props)
		if not obj or not obj.Parent then return end
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(t, style, dir), props):Play()
	end

	local function getCharacter() return LocalPlayer.Character end

	local function getHumanoid(char)
		char = char or getCharacter()
		return char and char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
	end

	local function isAlive(char)
		char = char or getCharacter()
		local hum = getHumanoid(char)
		return char ~= nil and hum ~= nil and hum.Health > 0
	end

	-- Returns every Motor6D and Weld in the character, including inside held tools.
	local function getAllJoints(char)
		local joints = {}
		for _, v in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("Motor6D") or v:IsA("Weld") then
				table.insert(joints, v)
			end
		end
		return joints
	end

	-- ── Rig detection ─────────────────────────────────────────────
	-- R6 characters have a "Torso"; R15 have "UpperTorso".
	-- Knowing the rig lets us handle the RootJoint (R6) and HipRigAttachment
	-- (R15) correctly when rewiring joints.
	local function detectRigType(char)
		if char:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") then return "R15" end
		if char:FindFirstChild("Torso")      then return "R6"  end
		return "R15"
	end

	-- ── Network ownership ─────────────────────────────────────────
	-- Tries two methods to give the client physics authority over a part.
	-- Without this, the server may fight our CFrame writes on oldRoot,
	-- causing it to snap back to its last authoritative position.
	local function claimNetworkOwnership(part)
		pcall(function()
			if sethiddenproperty then
				sethiddenproperty(part, "NetworkOwnershipRule",
					Enum.NetworkOwnershipRule.Manual)
			end
		end)
		pcall(function()
			-- SetNetworkOwner is server-only in the API, but some executors
			-- expose it client-side through raw method access.
			part:SetNetworkOwner(LocalPlayer)
		end)
	end

	-- ── Slider ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function setButtonState(state)
		if not sliderFrame then return end
		local pos = (state == "on")
			and UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
			or  UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
		Tween(sliderFrame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out,
			{ Position = pos })
	end

	-- ── Godmode ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function applyGodmodeHooks(char)
		if not (getrawmetatable and setreadonly and newcclosure) then return end
		local hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 5)
		if not hum then return end
		local ok, err = pcall(function()
			local mt    = getrawmetatable(game)
			local oldNC = mt.__namecall
			local oldNI = mt.__newindex
			setreadonly(mt, false)
			mt.__namecall = newcclosure(function(self, ...)
				local m = getnamecallmethod()
				if self == hum then
					if m == "ChangeState" and select(1,...) == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead then return end
					if m == "SetStateEnabled" then
						local st, en = ...
						if st == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead and en == true then return end
					end
					if m == "Destroy" then return end
				end
				if self == char and m == "BreakJoints" then return end
				return oldNC(self, ...)
			end)
			mt.__newindex = newcclosure(function(self, k, v)
				if self == hum then
					if k == "Health"             and type(v)=="number" and v<=0            then return end
					if k == "MaxHealth"          and type(v)=="number" and v<hum.MaxHealth then return end
					if k == "BreakJointsOnDeath" and v==true                               then return end
					if k == "Parent"             and v==nil                                then return end
				end
				return oldNI(self, k, v)
			end)
			setreadonly(mt, true)
		end)
		if not ok then warn("[SemiInvis] Godmode hook failed:", err) end
	end

	local function setupGodmode()
		local char = getCharacter()
		if char then applyGodmodeHooks(char) end
		if not godmodeApplied then
			godmodeApplied = true
			Maid:Add("Godmode", LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(applyGodmodeHooks))
		end
	end

	-- ── removeFolders ─────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function removeFolders()
		local playerFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name)
		if not playerFolder then return end
		for _, name in ipairs({"DoubleRig","Constraints"}) do
			local f = playerFolder:FindFirstChild(name)
			if f then f:Destroy() end
		end
		Maid:Add("InvisCore", playerFolder.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
			if child.Name == "DoubleRig" or child.Name == "Constraints" then
				child:Destroy()
			end
		end))
	end

	-- ── doClone ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function doClone()
		local char = getCharacter()
		if not isAlive(char) then return false end
		local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not root then return false end

		rigType = detectRigType(char)
		hip     = char.Humanoid.HipHeight
		oldRoot = root

		local tmp  = Instance.new("Model")
		tmp.Parent = game
		char.Parent = tmp

		clone        = root:Clone()
		clone.Name   = "HumanoidRootPart"
		clone.Parent = char

		root.Parent     = Camera
		root.CanCollide = false
		root.CanTouch   = false
		root.CFrame     = clone.CFrame

		char.PrimaryPart = clone
		char.Parent      = Workspace

		-- Generic rewire for all Motor6D / Welds
		for _, v in ipairs(getAllJoints(char)) do
			if v.Part0 == oldRoot then v.Part0 = clone end
			if v.Part1 == oldRoot then v.Part1 = clone end
		end

		-- R6 extra: the RootJoint connecting Torso to HRP lives on Torso,
		-- not on HRP itself, so the generic loop won't always catch it.
		if rigType == "R6" then
			local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso")
			if torso then
				local rj = torso:FindFirstChild("RootJoint")
				if rj and rj.Part0 == oldRoot then rj.Part0 = clone end
			end
		end

		claimNetworkOwnership(root)

		tmp:Destroy()
		return true
	end

	-- ── revertClone ───────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function revertClone()
		if not oldRoot then return false end
		if not oldRoot:IsDescendantOf(Camera) then
			warn("[SemiInvis] revertClone: oldRoot not in Camera — clearing refs")
			oldRoot = nil; clone = nil
			return false
		end

		local char = getCharacter()
		if not isAlive(char) then
			if clone and clone.Parent then clone:Destroy() end
			clone = nil; oldRoot.Parent = nil; oldRoot = nil
			return false
		end

		local tmp  = Instance.new("Model")
		tmp.Parent = game
		char.Parent = tmp

		oldRoot.Parent   = char
		char.PrimaryPart = oldRoot
		char.Parent      = Workspace

		oldRoot.CanCollide = true
		oldRoot.CanTouch   = true

		for _, v in ipairs(getAllJoints(char)) do
			if v.Part0 == clone then v.Part0 = oldRoot end
			if v.Part1 == clone then v.Part1 = oldRoot end
		end

		if rigType == "R6" then
			local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso")
			if torso then
				local rj = torso:FindFirstChild("RootJoint")
				if rj and rj.Part0 == clone then rj.Part0 = oldRoot end
			end
		end

		if clone then
			oldRoot.CFrame = clone.CFrame
			clone:Destroy()
			clone = nil
		end

		if char.Humanoid then char.Humanoid.HipHeight = hip end
		oldRoot = nil
		tmp:Destroy()
		return true
	end

	-- ── Animation fallback chain ──────────────────────────────────
	-- Iterates Config.AnimationIds until one loads successfully.
	-- This matters on games that block specific asset IDs server-side.
	local function loadAnimationWithFallback(animator)
		for _, id in ipairs(Config.AnimationIds) do
			local ok, track = pcall(function()
				local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
				anim.AnimationId = id
				local t = animator:LoadAnimation(anim)
				anim:Destroy()
				return t
			end)
			if ok and track then
				return track
			else
				warn("[SemiInvis] Animation", id, "failed, trying next fallback")
			end
		end
		warn("[SemiInvis] All animation fallbacks exhausted")
		return nil
	end

	-- ── animationTrickery ─────────────────────────────────────────
	local function animationTrickery()
		local char = getCharacter()
		if not isAlive(char) then return end

		if animTrack then
			pcall(function() animTrack:Stop(0); animTrack:Destroy() end)
			animTrack = nil
		end
		Maid:Clean("InvisAnim")

		local hum      = char.Humanoid
		local animator = hum:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Animator")
			or Instance.new("Animator", hum)

		animTrack = loadAnimationWithFallback(animator)
		if not animTrack then return end

		animTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4
		animTrack:Play(0, 1, 0)

		Maid:Add("InvisAnim", animTrack.Stopped:Connect(function()
			if isInvisible then animationTrickery() end
		end))

		task.defer(function()
			if animTrack and animTrack.IsPlaying then
				animTrack.TimePosition = 0.7
				task.wait(1)
				if animTrack and animTrack.IsPlaying then
					animTrack:AdjustSpeed(math.huge)
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	-- ── Tool weld re-wiring ───────────────────────────────────────
	-- Tools equipped mid-session contain Motor6D joints that reference the
	-- real HRP. DescendantAdded fires when the tool lands in the character;
	-- we defer one frame so all its joints are present before patching.
	local function patchDescendantJoint(inst)
		if not (clone and oldRoot) then return end
		if inst:IsA("Motor6D") or inst:IsA("Weld") then
			if inst.Part0 == oldRoot then inst.Part0 = clone end
			if inst.Part1 == oldRoot then inst.Part1 = clone end
		end
	end

	local function startToolWatcher(char)
		Maid:Add("InvisCore", char.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(desc)
			task.defer(function() patchDescendantJoint(desc) end)
		end))
	end

	-- ── Health watcher ────────────────────────────────────────────
	-- Some anti-cheat systems or server scripts reset the character model,
	-- which breaks the clone arrangement. This watcher checks integrity on
	-- a timer and silently reapplies if something is wrong.
	local function startHealthWatcher()
		task.spawn(function()
			while isInvisible do
				task.wait(Config.WatcherInterval)
				if not isInvisible then break end

				local char   = getCharacter()
				local broken = false

				if not oldRoot or not oldRoot:IsDescendantOf(Camera) then
					broken = true
				elseif not clone or not clone.Parent or not clone:IsDescendantOf(char or game) then
					broken = true
				elseif char and char.PrimaryPart ~= clone then
					broken = true
				end

				if broken then
					warn("[SemiInvis] Integrity check failed — reapplying")
					if animTrack then
						pcall(function() animTrack:Stop(0); animTrack:Destroy() end)
						animTrack = nil
					end
					Maid:Clean("InvisAnim")
					clone = nil; oldRoot = nil  -- state is broken; don't try revertClone

					local ok = doClone()
					if ok then
						task.wait(0.1)
						animationTrickery()
						removeFolders()
					else
						warn("[SemiInvis] Reapply failed — disabling")
						isInvisible = false
						setButtonState("off")
						break
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	-- ── Full cleanup ──────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function fullCleanup()
		if animTrack then
			pcall(function() animTrack:Stop(0); animTrack:Destroy() end)
			animTrack = nil
		end
		Maid:Clean("InvisCore")
		Maid:Clean("InvisAnim")
		pcall(revertClone)
		removeFolders()
	end

	-- ── enableInvisibility ────────────────────────────────────────
	local function enableInvisibility()
		local char = getCharacter()
		if not isAlive(char) then return false end

		removeFolders()
		if not doClone() then return false end

		task.wait(0.1)
		animationTrickery()
		startToolWatcher(char)
		startHealthWatcher()

		-- PreSimulation: position the hidden root every physics step
		Maid:Add("InvisCore", RunService.PreSimulation:Connect(function()
			if not oldRoot or not isAlive() then return end
			local root = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart
			if not root then return end

			if Config.HitboxStrategy == "REMOTE" then
				-- Bury the hitbox far underground so server raycasts miss entirely
				oldRoot.CFrame = CFrame.new(root.Position.X, -5000, root.Position.Z)
			else
				-- SINK: position under clone with a tiny random jitter each frame
				local hum    = getHumanoid()
				local jitter = (math.random() * 2 - 1) * Config.SinkJitter
				local sinkY  = (hum and hum.HipHeight or 2) + (root.Size.Y / 2) - 1 + Config.SinkOffset + jitter
				oldRoot.CFrame = (root.CFrame - Vector3.new(0, sinkY, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(180), 0, 0)
			end

			oldRoot.AssemblyLinearVelocity = root.AssemblyLinearVelocity
		end))

		-- Auto-disable on death
		local hum = getHumanoid(char)
		if hum then
			Maid:Add("InvisCore", hum.Died:Connect(function()
				if not isInvisible then return end
				isInvisible = false
				setButtonState("off")
				fullCleanup()
			end))
		end

		-- Handle respawn
		Maid:Add("InvisCore", LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
			if not isInvisible then return end
			isInvisible = false
			setButtonState("off")
			animTrack = nil; clone = nil; oldRoot = nil
			Maid:Clean("InvisCore")
			Maid:Clean("InvisAnim")
		end))

		return true
	end

	-- ── toggle ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function toggle()
		if isToggling then return end
		isToggling = true

		isInvisible = not isInvisible

		if isInvisible then
			setupGodmode()
			local ok = enableInvisibility()
			if not ok then
				isInvisible = false
				fullCleanup()
				setButtonState("off")
			else
				setButtonState("on")
			end
		else
			fullCleanup()
			setButtonState("off")
		end

		task.delay(Config.ToggleCooldown, function() isToggling = false end)
	end

	-- ── Input ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end
		local bindText = bindButton.Text
		if bindText == "..." or bindText == "" then return end
		local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
		if ok and kc and input.KeyCode == kc then toggle() end
	end)

	-- ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	setButtonState("off")
end;
task.spawn(C_33);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.3.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_44()
	local script = G2L["44"];
	-- ANTI RAGDOLL, EFFECTS & KNOCKBACK
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Prevents visual ragdoll, keeps character walkable, and kills all knockback velocity

	if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

	local Players           = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService        = game:GetService("RunService")
	local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	local TweenService      = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService  = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled      = false
	local DisabledRemotes = {}
	local RemoteWatcher  = nil
	local steppedConn    = nil
	local descendantConn = nil

	-- Any velocity spike above this (studs/s) is treated as knockback and zeroed
	-- Set higher if normal movement feels affected, lower for stricter blocking
	local KNOCKBACK_THRESHOLD = 50

	local BAD_STATES = {
		[Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll]     = true,
		[Enum.HumanoidStateType.FallingDown] = true,
		[Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics]     = true,
		[Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead]        = true,
	}
	local RemoteKeywords = { "useitem", "combatservice", "ragdoll", "knockback", "launch", "blast" }

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	-- Motor6D ON  → limbs stay attached and play animations normally
	-- Constraints OFF → ragdoll physics can't fling limbs around
	local function enforceJoints(character)
		for _, v in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("Motor6D") then
				v.Enabled = true
			elseif v:IsA("BallSocketConstraint")
				or v:IsA("HingeConstraint")
				or v:IsA("Constraint")
			then
				v.Enabled = false
			end
		end
	end

	-- Bring humanoid back to a walkable running state WITHOUT anchoring HRP
	local function forceWalkable(character)
		local hum = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not hum or not hrp then return end

		if hum.Health <= 0 then hum.Health = hum.MaxHealth end

		if BAD_STATES[hum:GetState()] then
			hrp.Anchored = false
			hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
		end
	end

	-- Anti-knockback: detect sudden unnatural velocity spikes and zero them out
	-- We check AssemblyLinearVelocity on the HRP. The player's normal movement
	-- speed is well below the threshold so legitimate movement is untouched.
	-- We preserve the Y component only when the player is naturally falling,
	-- otherwise a jumping character would feel stuttery.
	local function antiKnockback(character)
		local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local hum = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if not hrp or not hum then return end

		local vel = hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity
		local horizontalSpeed = Vector3.new(vel.X, 0, vel.Z).Magnitude

		if horizontalSpeed > KNOCKBACK_THRESHOLD then
			-- Zero horizontal knockback, preserve vertical so gravity still works
			hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, math.min(vel.Y, 0), 0)
		end

		-- Also kill angular (spin) knockback every frame
		if hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity.Magnitude > 0.1 then
			hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
		end
	end

	local function InitAntiRagdoll(character)
		local hum = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
		if not hum then return end

		-- Block bad states up front
		for state in pairs(BAD_STATES) do
			hum:SetStateEnabled(state, false)
		end

		-- Kill any ragdoll constraints injected at runtime (games add these on hit)
		if descendantConn then descendantConn:Disconnect() end
		descendantConn = character.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(v)
			if not isEnabled then return end
			task.defer(function()
				if not v or not v.Parent then return end
				if v:IsA("BallSocketConstraint") or v:IsA("HingeConstraint") or v:IsA("Constraint") then
					v.Enabled = false
				elseif v:IsA("Motor6D") then
					v.Enabled = true
				end
			end)
		end)

		-- React instantly when a bad state sneaks through
		hum.StateChanged:Connect(function(_, new)
			if not isEnabled then return end
			if BAD_STATES[new] then
				enforceJoints(character)
				forceWalkable(character)
				-- Also immediately zero velocity since state changes often coincide with a knockback
				local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if hrp then
					hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity  = Vector3.zero
					hrp.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
				end
			end
		end)

		-- Main enforcement loop — every physics step
		if steppedConn then steppedConn:Disconnect() end
		steppedConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			enforceJoints(character)
			forceWalkable(character)
			antiKnockback(character)
			if hum.Health < hum.MaxHealth then
				hum.Health = hum.MaxHealth
			end
		end)
	end

	-- Block client-side remote connections for ragdoll/knockback/UseItem effects
	local function KillRemote(remote)
		if not getconnections then return end
		if not remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end
		if DisabledRemotes[remote] then return end
		local name = remote.Name:lower()
		for _, key in ipairs(RemoteKeywords) do
			if name:find(key) then
				DisabledRemotes[remote] = {}
				pcall(function()
					for _, c in ipairs(getconnections(remote.OnClientEvent)) do
						if c.Disable then
							c:Disable()
							table.insert(DisabledRemotes[remote], c)
						end
					end
				end)
				break
			end
		end
	end

	local function InitAntiItem()
		pcall(function()
			local PM = require(Player:WaitForChild("PlayerScripts"):WaitForChild("PlayerModule"))
			PM:GetControls():Enable()
		end)
		for _, obj in ipairs(ReplicatedStorage:GetDescendants()) do KillRemote(obj) end
		if RemoteWatcher then RemoteWatcher:Disconnect() end
		RemoteWatcher = ReplicatedStorage.DescendantAdded:Connect(KillRemote)
	end

	local function ReEnableRemotes()
		for _, conns in pairs(DisabledRemotes) do
			for _, c in ipairs(conns) do pcall(function() c:Enable() end) end
		end
		DisabledRemotes = {}
		if RemoteWatcher then RemoteWatcher:Disconnect(); RemoteWatcher = nil end
	end

	local function disableAll()
		if steppedConn    then steppedConn:Disconnect();    steppedConn = nil end
		if descendantConn then descendantConn:Disconnect(); descendantConn = nil end
		ReEnableRemotes()

		local char = Player.Character
		if char then
			local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if hum then
				for state in pairs(BAD_STATES) do
					hum:SetStateEnabled(state, true)
				end
			end
			for _, v in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
				if v:IsA("Motor6D") then v.Enabled = true end
			end
		end
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			local char = Player.Character
			if char then InitAntiRagdoll(char) end
			task.delay(0.25, InitAntiItem)
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableAll()
		end
	end

	Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
		task.wait(0.4)
		if isEnabled then InitAntiRagdoll(char) end
	end)

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_44);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.4.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_56()
	local script = G2L["56"];
	-- FLOAT
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Floats the player in place using AssemblyLinearVelocity + BodyGyro

	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false
	local floatConn = nil
	local bodyGyro = nil
	local floatHeight = nil  -- saved Y when enabled

	local FLOAT_SPEED   = 30   -- horizontal movement speed while floating
	local FLOAT_LIFT    = 40   -- upward force (counters gravity effectively)
	local FLOAT_GRAVITY = workspace.Gravity

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	local function getChar()
		return LocalPlayer.Character
	end

	local function enableFloat()
		local char = getChar()
		if not char then return end
		local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if not hrp or not hum then return end

		floatHeight = hrp.Position.Y

		-- Add a BodyGyro to keep the character upright
		bodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro")
		bodyGyro.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
		bodyGyro.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
		bodyGyro.D = 100
		bodyGyro.P = 10000
		bodyGyro.Parent = hrp

		floatConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			local c = getChar()
			if not c then return end
			local root = c:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			local h = c:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if not root or not h then return end

			local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera
			local move = Vector3.zero

			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then
				move += cam.CFrame.LookVector
			end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then
				move -= cam.CFrame.LookVector
			end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then
				move += cam.CFrame.RightVector
			end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then
				move -= cam.CFrame.RightVector
			end

			-- Flatten horizontal movement
			move = Vector3.new(move.X, 0, move.Z)
			if move.Magnitude > 0 then move = move.Unit end

			-- Vertical control
			local verticalVel = 0
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then
				verticalVel = FLOAT_LIFT
				floatHeight = root.Position.Y
			elseif UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftAlt) then
				verticalVel = -FLOAT_LIFT
				floatHeight = root.Position.Y
			else
				-- Hover: push toward saved float height
				local diff = floatHeight - root.Position.Y
				verticalVel = math.clamp(diff * 10, -FLOAT_LIFT, FLOAT_LIFT)
			end

			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = move * FLOAT_SPEED + Vector3.new(0, verticalVel, 0)
			h:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall, false)
			h:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping, false)
		end)
	end

	local function disableFloat()
		if floatConn then floatConn:Disconnect(); floatConn = nil end
		if bodyGyro then bodyGyro:Destroy(); bodyGyro = nil end

		local char = getChar()
		if char then
			local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			local hum = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if hrp then hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero end
			if hum then
				hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall, true)
				hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping, true)
			end
		end
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			enableFloat()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableFloat()
		end
	end

	-- Reset on respawn
	LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
		if isEnabled then
			disableFloat()
			task.wait(1)
			enableFloat()
		end
	end)

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_56);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.5.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_67()
	local script = G2L["67"];
	-- GRAPPLE FLY (MODIFIED SPEED)
	-- script.Parent = TextButton

	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
	local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false

	local FLY_SPEED = 50

	local flyConn = nil
	local remoteSpamConn = nil
	local toolEquipped = false

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	local function getCharParts()
		local char = LocalPlayer.Character
		if not char then return nil, nil, nil end
		return char, char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"), char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	end

	local function equipTool()
		local _, _, hum = getCharParts()
		local tool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Grapple Hook")
		if tool and hum and not toolEquipped then
			hum:EquipTool(tool)
			toolEquipped = true
		end
	end

	local function startRemoteSpam()
		if remoteSpamConn then return end
		remoteSpamConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			pcall(function()
				ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Net["RE/UseItem"]:FireServer(FLY_SPEED)
			end)
		end)
	end

	local function stopRemoteSpam()
		if remoteSpamConn then remoteSpamConn:Disconnect(); remoteSpamConn = nil end
	end

	local function enableFly()
		local char, hrp, hum = getCharParts()
		if not char or not hrp or not hum then return end

		equipTool()
		startRemoteSpam()

		flyConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			local c, root, h = getCharParts()
			if not c or not root then return end

			local tool = c:FindFirstChild("Grapple Hook")
			if not tool then
				toolEquipped = false
				equipTool()
			end

			local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera
			local move = Vector3.zero

			-- Controls
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then move += cam.CFrame.LookVector end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then move -= cam.CFrame.LookVector end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then move += cam.CFrame.RightVector end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then move -= cam.CFrame.RightVector end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then move += Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
			if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) then move -= Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end

			-- Mobile support
			pcall(function()
				local PlayerModule = LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:FindFirstChild("PlayerModule")
				if PlayerModule then
					local ControlModule = require(PlayerModule:WaitForChild("ControlModule"))
					local moveVector = ControlModule:GetMoveVector()
					if moveVector.Magnitude > 0 then
						move += (cam.CFrame.LookVector * -moveVector.Z + cam.CFrame.RightVector * moveVector.X)
					end
				end
			end)

			if move.Magnitude > 0 then
				move = move.Unit
				root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = move * FLY_SPEED
			else
				root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
			end
		end)
	end

	local function disableFly()
		if flyConn then flyConn:Disconnect(); flyConn = nil end
		stopRemoteSpam()
		toolEquipped = false

		local char, hrp = getCharParts()
		if hrp then hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero end
		if char then
			local tool = char:FindFirstChild("Grapple Hook")
			if tool then tool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack end
		end
	end

	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			enableFly()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableFly()
		end
	end

	LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
		toolEquipped = false
		if isEnabled then
			disableFly()
			isEnabled = false
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
		end
	end)

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_67);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.6.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_78()
	local script = G2L["78"];
	-- PLATFORM INF JUMP (NO FLING / NO CLIP)

	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- bind system
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local txt = bindButton.Text
			if txt == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[txt] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false
	local platform = nil
	local busy = false

	local BOOST_HEIGHT = 7
	local BOOST_TIME = 0.12

	-- how far BELOW HRP the platform sits
	local OFFSET = 4.2  -- <- important (prevents clipping)

	local function Tween(obj, t, style, dir, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(t, style, dir), props):Play()
	end

	local function getRoot()
		local char = LocalPlayer.Character
		return char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	end

	local function ensurePlatform()
		if platform then return end

		platform = Instance.new("Part")
		platform.Size = Vector3.new(6,1,6)
		platform.Anchored = true
		platform.CanCollide = false
		platform.Transparency = 0.3
		platform.Name = "1283492349u1h2h3tjib13 q3189rt h2oqebr0892qhfi1npih1q3gnpirntgwd"
		platform.Parent = workspace
	end

	local function doBoost()
		if busy then return end
		busy = true

		local root = getRoot()
		if not root then busy = false return end

		ensurePlatform()

		-- position safely BELOW player (no overlap)
		local baseCF = root.CFrame - Vector3.new(0, OFFSET, 0)
		platform.CFrame = baseCF
		platform.CanCollide = true

		-- APPLY CLEAN UPWARD VELOCITY (prevents physics fling)
		root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.X,
			60, -- upward force
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Z
		)

		-- small visual lift for the platform
		Tween(platform, BOOST_TIME, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
			CFrame = baseCF + Vector3.new(0, BOOST_HEIGHT, 0)
		})

		-- disable collision quickly so you fall naturally
		task.delay(0.08, function()
			if platform then
				platform.CanCollide = false
			end
		end)

		-- cooldown
		task.delay(BOOST_TIME, function()
			busy = false
		end)
	end

	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled

		if isEnabled then
			Tween(button.Frame,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{
				Position = UDim2.new(0.75,0,0.5,0)
			})
		else
			Tween(button.Frame,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{
				Position = UDim2.new(0.25,0,0.5,0)
			})
			if platform then
				platform:Destroy()
				platform = nil
			end
		end
	end

	-- jump trigger
	UserInputService.JumpRequest:Connect(function()
		if not isEnabled then return end
		doBoost()
	end)

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input,gp)
		if gp then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)

	LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
		if platform then
			platform:Destroy()
			platform = nil
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_78);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.1.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_89()
	local script = G2L["89"];
	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end
	-- Services
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	-- References
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent
	local bindButton = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")

	-- Config
	local CHECK_INTERVAL = 0.5 -- seconds between scans

	-- State
	local enabled = false
	local connection
	local lastCheck = 0

	-- Position resolver
	local function getPos(obj)
		if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
			return obj.Position
		elseif obj:IsA("Model") then
			if obj.PrimaryPart then
				return obj.PrimaryPart.Position
			else
				local cf = obj:GetBoundingBox()
				return cf.Position
			end
		elseif obj:IsA("Attachment") then
			return obj.WorldPosition
		end
		return nil
	end

	-- Find closest Steal prompt
	local function getClosestPrompt()
		local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
		local root = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

		local closest, dist = nil, math.huge

		for _, v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and v.ActionText == "Steal" then
				local pos = getPos(v.Parent)
				if pos then
					local d = (root.Position - pos).Magnitude
					if d < dist then
						dist = d
						closest = v
					end
				end
			end
		end

		return closest
	end

	-- Start the auto loop
	local function start()
		if connection then return end
		lastCheck = 0

		connection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
			if not enabled then return end

			lastCheck += dt
			if lastCheck < CHECK_INTERVAL then return end
			lastCheck = 0

			local prompt = getClosestPrompt()
			if prompt then
				fireproximityprompt(prompt)
			end
		end)
	end

	-- Stop the auto loop
	local function stop()
		if connection then
			connection:Disconnect()
			connection = nil
		end
	end

	-- Toggle function
	local function toggle()
		enabled = not enabled

		if enabled then
			start()
			Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
				Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
			})
		else
			stop()
			Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
				Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
			})
		end
	end

	-- Mouse click toggle
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	-- Keybind toggle
	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end

		local keyText = bindButton.Text
		if keyText == "..." then return end -- unbound

		local keyEnum = Enum.KeyCode[keyText:upper()]
		if keyEnum and input.KeyCode == keyEnum then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_89);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.2.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_9a()
	local script = G2L["9a"];
	-- ANTI EFFECTS
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Removes all visual effects, locks FOV to 70, and clears fog/glow/particles

	local Players          = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService       = game:GetService("RunService")
	local Lighting         = game:GetService("Lighting")
	local TweenService     = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	local button = script.Parent

	local FOV_LOCK = 70

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton     = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false
	local fovConn         = nil
	local lightingConn    = nil

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	-- Full list of blacklisted effect class names
	local blacklist = {
		"BlurEffect", "ColorCorrectionEffect", "BloomEffect", "SunRaysEffect",
		"DepthOfFieldEffect", "Atmosphere", "Sky", "Smoke", "ParticleEmitter",
		"Beam", "Trail", "Highlight", "PostEffect", "SurfaceAppearance",
		"Fire", "Sparkles", "Explosion", "PointLight", "SpotLight", "SurfaceLight",
		"Shadows", "Blur", "Fog", "ColorGradingEffect", "ToneMappingEffect",
		"VignetteEffect", "GodRays", "Glare", "ChromaticAberrationEffect",
		"DistortionEffect", "LensFlare", "SunFlare", "LightInfluence",
		"AmbientOcclusionEffect", "RefractionEffect", "HeatDistortion",
		"GlitchEffect", "ScreenSpaceReflection", "MotionBlur", "VolumetricLight",
		"RainEffect", "SnowEffect", "LightningEffect", "NeonGlow",
		"ContrastCorrection", "ShadowMap", "Bloom", "Clouds", "FogVolume",
		"WaterEffect", "WindEffect", "PixelateEffect", "FilmGrainEffect",
		"CRTShader", "NightVisionEffect", "InfraredEffect", "HazeEffect",
		"ColorBalanceEffect", "DynamicLight", "AmbientEffect", "ScreenDistortion",
		"ScanlineEffect", "UnderwaterEffect", "ThermalVision", "ShockwaveEffect",
		"FlashEffect", "ExplosionLight", "VFXPart", "GlitchScreen",
		"ScreenFlash", "OverlayEffect", "ShadowEffect", "GhostEffect",
		"FogEmitter", "WindEmitter", "HeatWave", "SunGlow", "ColorOverlay",
		"VisionDistort", "EchoEffect", "ScreenOverlay", "RenderEffect",
		"VisualEffect", "LightingEffect", "CameraEffect", "WeatherEffect",
		"SmokeTrail", "FireTrail", "NeonEffect", "RefractionLayer",
		"PostProcessingEffect", "VisualNoise", "ScreenNoise",
	}

	local function isBlacklisted(obj)
		for _, name in ipairs(blacklist) do
			if obj:IsA(name) then return true end
		end
		return false
	end

	local function clearEffects()
		for _, v in ipairs(Lighting:GetDescendants()) do
			if isBlacklisted(v) then
				pcall(function() v:Destroy() end)
			end
		end
		-- Also clear effects from workspace (particles on parts, etc.)
		for _, v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
			if isBlacklisted(v) then
				pcall(function() v:Destroy() end)
			end
		end
	end

	local function enableAntiEffects()
		-- Initial sweep
		clearEffects()

		-- Watch Lighting for new effects being added
		lightingConn = Lighting.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
			task.wait()
			if isBlacklisted(obj) then
				pcall(function() obj:Destroy() end)
			end
		end)

		-- Lock FOV every render step
		fovConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			if camera.FieldOfView ~= FOV_LOCK then
				camera.FieldOfView = FOV_LOCK
			end
		end)
	end

	local function disableAntiEffects()
		if fovConn      then fovConn:Disconnect();      fovConn = nil      end
		if lightingConn then lightingConn:Disconnect(); lightingConn = nil end
		-- Restore default FOV
		camera.FieldOfView = 70  -- Roblox default; adjust if your game uses a different default
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			enableAntiEffects()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableAntiEffects()
		end
	end

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_9a);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.FeaturesFrame.9.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_ab()
	local script = G2L["ab"];
	-- BALLOON ON RESET
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Monitors the local player's head size every RenderStepped.
	-- If a suspicious balloon head size is detected, it nukes the character (forces respawn).

	local Players          = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService       = game:GetService("RunService")
	local TweenService     = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton     = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then
				currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false
	local renderConn = nil

	-- Suspicious balloon head sizes from source
	local headSizesToCheck = {
		Vector3.new(2.395698070526123, 2.395698070526123, 2.395698070526123),
		Vector3.new(2.4048495292663574, 2.4048495292663574, 2.4048495292663574),
	}
	local TOLERANCE = 0.5  -- studs; how close the head size needs to be to trigger

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	local function isHeadSizeSuspicious(head)
		for _, targetSize in ipairs(headSizesToCheck) do
			local dx = math.abs(head.Size.X - targetSize.X)
			local dy = math.abs(head.Size.Y - targetSize.Y)
			local dz = math.abs(head.Size.Z - targetSize.Z)
			if dx <= TOLERANCE and dy <= TOLERANCE and dz <= TOLERANCE then
				return true
			end
		end
		return false
	end

	local function enableBalloonReset()
		renderConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			local char = player.Character
			if char and char:FindFirstChild("Head") then
				if isHeadSizeSuspicious(char.Head) then
					-- Nuke the character to force a respawn (same as source)
					char:ClearAllChildren()
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	local function disableBalloonReset()
		if renderConn then renderConn:Disconnect(); renderConn = nil end
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			enableBalloonReset()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableBalloonReset()
		end
	end

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then
			toggle()
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_ab);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.Frame.ImageLabel.LocalScript
local function C_b4()
	local script = G2L["b4"];
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local player = Players.LocalPlayer

	local imageLabel = script.Parent

	-- function to update the image
	local function updateImage()
		local userId = player.UserId
		local thumbType = Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot
		local thumbSize = Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420

		local content, isReady = Players:GetUserThumbnailAsync(userId, thumbType, thumbSize)
		imageLabel.Image = content
	end

	-- run once
	updateImage()

	-- also update if character reloads (optional)
	player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
		updateImage()
	end)

end;
task.spawn(C_b4);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.Frame.TextLabel.LocalScript
local function C_b8()
	local script = G2L["b8"];
	local Players = game:GetService("Players")
	local TextService = game:GetService("TextService")

	local player = Players.LocalPlayer
	local label = script.Parent

	local function getFittingText(fullText)
		local maxWidth = label.AbsoluteSize.X
		local font = label.Font
		local textSize = label.TextSize

		-- if it already fits, return it
		local textBounds = TextService:GetTextSize(fullText, textSize, font, Vector2.new(1e6, 1e6))
		if textBounds.X <= maxWidth then
			return fullText
		end

		-- otherwise trim until it fits with "..."
		for i = #fullText, 1, -1 do
			local shortened = string.sub(fullText, 1, i) .. "..."
			local bounds = TextService:GetTextSize(shortened, textSize, font, Vector2.new(1e6, 1e6))

			if bounds.X <= maxWidth then
				return shortened
			end
		end

		return "..."
	end

	local function updateText()
		local full =  "@" .. player.Name
		label.Text = getFittingText(full)
	end

	-- run once
	updateText()

	-- update if display name changes
	player:GetPropertyChangedSignal("DisplayName"):Connect(updateText)

	-- update if UI size changes (IMPORTANT for scaled UI)
	label:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteSize"):Connect(updateText)

end;
task.spawn(C_b8);
