	-- Fake Module Scripts:
	
	local fake_module_scripts = {}
	
	
	-- Fake Local Scripts:
	
	local function NKHHVX_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.drag
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "drag"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_Frame"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local gui = script.Parent -- the GUI you want to drag
		local dragging = false
		local dragStart = nil
		local startPos = nil
		
		-- When the player clicks the GUI
		gui.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
			if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
				dragging = true
				dragStart = input.Position
				startPos = gui.Position
		
				-- Capture input so we can track when the mouse moves outside GUI
				input.Changed:Connect(function()
					if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
						dragging = false
					end
				end)
			end
		end)
		
		-- When the player moves the mouse
		gui.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
			if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement and dragging then
				local delta = input.Position - dragStart
				gui.Position = UDim2.new(
					startPos.X.Scale,
					startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
					startPos.Y.Scale,
					startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
				)
			end
		end)
		
	end
	local function ICJOPF_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.borderStrke.borderGrandient.swift
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "swift"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_borderGrandient"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local uiGradient = script.Parent
		local tweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		
		local gradientTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
			2,
			Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
			Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
			-1,
			false,
			0
		)
		
		tweenService:Create(uiGradient, gradientTweenInfo, {Rotation = 360}):Play()
	end
	local function LLCQ_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.AutoDuelFrame.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_AutoDuelFrame"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		-- -- Auto Duel Script (Single-Run Version) -- --
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
		local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
		
		local frame = script.Parent
		local leftBtn  = frame:WaitForChild("left")
		local rightBtn = frame:WaitForChild("right")
		local kb1Btn   = frame:WaitForChild("keybind1")
		local kb2Btn   = frame:WaitForChild("keybind2")
		
		-- ─── Keybind Save / Load ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local JSON_FILE = "keybind_autoduel.json"
		local keybinds = { left = Enum.KeyCode.X, right = Enum.KeyCode.Z }
		
		local function saveKeybinds()
			if writefile then
				pcall(writefile, JSON_FILE, HttpService:JSONEncode({
					left  = keybinds.left.Name,
					right = keybinds.right.Name,
				}))
			end
		end
		
		local function loadKeybinds()
			if isfile and isfile(JSON_FILE) then
				local ok, data = pcall(function()
					return HttpService:JSONDecode(readfile(JSON_FILE))
				end)
				if ok and data then
					if data.left  then local kc = Enum.KeyCode[data.left]  if kc then keybinds.left  = kc end end
					if data.right then local kc = Enum.KeyCode[data.right] if kc then keybinds.right = kc end end
				end
			end
		end
		
		loadKeybinds()
		kb1Btn.Text = keybinds.left.Name
		kb2Btn.Text = keybinds.right.Name
		
		-- ─── Keybind Listener UI ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local listeningFor = nil
		
		local function startListening(side)
			listeningFor = side
			if side == "left" then kb1Btn.Text = "..." else kb2Btn.Text = "..." end
		end
		
		kb1Btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() startListening("left")  end)
		kb2Btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() startListening("right") end)
		
		-- ─── Paths ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local LEFT_PATH = {
			{ position = Vector3.new(-475,-7,96),  speed = 59 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-483,-5,95),  speed = 59 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-487,-5,95),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-492,-5,95),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-473,-7,95),  speed = 29 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-473,-7,11),  speed = 29 },
		}
		
		local RIGHT_PATH = {
			{ position = Vector3.new(-474,-7,23),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-484,-5,24),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-488,-5,24),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-493,-5,25),  speed = 55 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-473,-7,25),  speed = 29 },
			{ position = Vector3.new(-474,-7,112), speed = 29 },
		}
		
		-- ─── Visual helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local COLOR_OFF  = Color3.fromRGB(77, 78, 97)
		local COLOR_ON   = Color3.fromRGB(60, 140, 60)
		
		local function setButtonColor(btn, color)
			btn.BackgroundColor3 = color
		end
		
		-- ─── State ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local activeConn    = nil   -- current RunService connection
		local isMoving      = false -- currently running a path
		
		-- ─── Stop helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local function stopMovement()
			if activeConn then
				activeConn:Disconnect()
				activeConn = nil
			end
			isMoving = false
			setButtonColor(leftBtn, COLOR_OFF)
			setButtonColor(rightBtn, COLOR_OFF)
		
			local char = LocalPlayer.Character
			local root = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if root then root.Velocity = Vector3.zero end
		end
		
		-- ─── Runner ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local function runPath(pathData, side)
			if isMoving then stopMovement() end
		
			isMoving = true
			if side == "left" then setButtonColor(leftBtn, COLOR_ON) else setButtonColor(rightBtn, COLOR_ON) end
		
			local idx     = 1
			local waiting = false
			local grabbed = false
		
			activeConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
				if waiting then return end
		
				local char = LocalPlayer.Character
				local root = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if not root then stopMovement() return end
		
				local wp = pathData[idx]
				if not wp then stopMovement() return end
		
				if (root.Position - wp.position).Magnitude < 5 then
					-- Pause at specific waypoints
					if (idx == 4 or idx == 6) and not grabbed then
						waiting = true
						root.Velocity = Vector3.zero
						task.delay(1.0, function()
							grabbed = true
							waiting = false
						end)
						return
					end
		
					if idx == #pathData then
						-- Path complete - just stop, don't trigger the other side
						stopMovement()
					else
						idx = idx + 1
						grabbed = false -- reset grab for next specific waypoint if needed
					end
				else
					local dir = (wp.position - root.Position).Unit
					root.Velocity = Vector3.new(dir.X * wp.speed, root.Velocity.Y, dir.Z * wp.speed)
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- ─── Input Logic ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		local function handleInput(side)
			if side == "left" then
				runPath(LEFT_PATH, "left")
			else
				runPath(RIGHT_PATH, "right")
			end
		end
		
		leftBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if listeningFor then return end
			handleInput("left")
		end)
		
		rightBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if listeningFor then return end
			handleInput("right")
		end)
		
		UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
			if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end
		
			if listeningFor then
				local kc = input.KeyCode
				keybinds[listeningFor] = kc
				if listeningFor == "left" then kb1Btn.Text = kc.Name else kb2Btn.Text = kc.Name end
				listeningFor = nil
				saveKeybinds()
				return
			end
		
			if gameProcessed then return end
		
			if input.KeyCode == keybinds.left then
				handleInput("left")
			elseif input.KeyCode == keybinds.right then
				handleInput("right")
			end
		end)
		
		-- ─── Init ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
		
		setButtonColor(leftBtn,  COLOR_OFF)
		setButtonColor(rightBtn, COLOR_OFF)
	end
	local function RAHG_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.Frame.SpinbotFrame.SwitchButton.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		--// SPIN CONTROLLER (improved coordination with stabilizer)
		
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")
		
		local player = Players.LocalPlayer
		local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
		local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
		local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
		local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		local align = rootPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("AlignOrientation")
		local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
			TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
		end
		local button = script.Parent
		local spinConnection
		local spinSpeed = 100
		local isSpinning = false
		
		local function startSpin()
			if spinConnection then return end
			isSpinning = true
		
			-- Disable stabilizer so it doesn't fight rotation
			if align then
				align.Enabled = false
			end
		
			-- Set AutoRotate to false so character controller doesn't override our spin
			humanoid.AutoRotate = false
		
			spinConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
				-- Continuously apply angular velocity
				rootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, spinSpeed, 0)
			end)
		end
		
		local function stopSpin()
			if spinConnection then
				spinConnection:Disconnect()
				spinConnection = nil
			end
		
			isSpinning = false
			rootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
		
			-- Re-enable AutoRotate so normal movement works
			humanoid.AutoRotate = true
		
			-- SNAP back to camera yaw so walking direction is correct
			if camera then
				local _, camYaw, _ = camera.CFrame:ToOrientation()
				rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(rootPart.Position) * CFrame.fromOrientation(0, camYaw, 0)
		
				-- Update the stabilizer's target immediately BEFORE re-enabling
				if align then
					align.CFrame = CFrame.fromOrientation(0, camYaw, 0)
				end
			end
		
			-- Small delay to let physics settle, then re-enable
			task.wait(0.05)
			if align and not isSpinning then
				align.Enabled = true
			end
		end
		
		script.Parent.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if script.Parent.Frame.Position == UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0) then
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
				startSpin()
			else
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
				stopSpin()
			end
		end)
	end
	local function HNLIBCB_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.Frame.AimbotFrame.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_AimbotFrame"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		-- Auto-Bat Detection Script
		-- Parent this script into the AimbotFrame
		
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
		
		-- Configuration
		local DETECTION_RADIUS = 5
		local DETECTION_HEIGHT = 3
		local BAT_COOLDOWN = 0.5
		local EQUIP_DELAY = 0.2
		
		-- State
		local Enabled = false
		local DetectionConnection = nil
		local DetectionPart = nil
		local LastBatActivation = 0
		local CurrentTarget = nil
		local isActivating = false
		
		-- Get references
		local TextButton = script.Parent:WaitForChild("SwitchButton")
		
		
		-- Function to create detection cylinder
		local function createDetectionCylinder()
			if DetectionPart then DetectionPart:Destroy() end
		
			local character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if not character then return end
		
			local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if not hrp then return end
		
			local cylinder = Instance.new("Part")
			cylinder.Name = "DetectionCylinder"
			cylinder.Shape = Enum.PartType.Cylinder
			cylinder.Size = Vector3.new(DETECTION_HEIGHT, DETECTION_RADIUS * 2, DETECTION_RADIUS * 2)
			cylinder.Transparency = 0.9
			cylinder.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0)
			cylinder.CanCollide = false
			cylinder.Anchored = true
			cylinder.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
			cylinder.Parent = workspace
		
			DetectionPart = cylinder
		
			local heartbeatConnection
			heartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				if not Enabled or not character or not character.Parent then
					if cylinder and cylinder.Parent then
						cylinder:Destroy()
					end
					if heartbeatConnection then
						heartbeatConnection:Disconnect()
					end
					return
				end
		
				if hrp and hrp.Parent then
					cylinder.CFrame = hrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -3, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(90))
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- Function to get equipped bat
		local function getEquippedBat()
			local character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if not character then return nil end
		
			local bat = character:FindFirstChild("Bat")
			if bat and bat:IsA("Tool") then
				return bat
			end
			return nil
		end
		
		-- Function to equip bat
		local function equipBat()
			local character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if not character then return false end
		
			local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if not humanoid then return false end
		
			local equippedBat = getEquippedBat()
			if equippedBat then return true end
		
			local bat = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Bat")
			if bat and bat:IsA("Tool") then
				humanoid:EquipTool(bat)
				return true
			end
		
			return false
		end
		
		-- Function to activate bat
		local function activateBat()
			local currentTime = tick()
		
			if currentTime - LastBatActivation < BAT_COOLDOWN then return false end
			if isActivating then return false end
		
			isActivating = true
			LastBatActivation = currentTime
		
			if not equipBat() then
				isActivating = false
				return false
			end
		
			task.delay(EQUIP_DELAY, function()
				local bat = getEquippedBat()
				if bat then
					bat:Activate()
				end
				isActivating = false
			end)
		
			return true
		end
		
		-- Function to face target
		local function faceTarget(targetPosition)
			local character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if not character then return end
		
			local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if not humanoid or not hrp then return end
		
			local direction = (targetPosition - hrp.Position)
			direction = Vector3.new(direction.X, 0, direction.Z)
			if direction.Magnitude > 0 then
				local nudgePos = hrp.Position + direction.Unit * 0.5
				humanoid:MoveTo(nudgePos)
			end
		end
		
		-- Function to find closest valid target
		local function findClosestTarget()
			local character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if not character then return nil end
		
			local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if not hrp then return nil end
		
			local closestPlayer = nil
			local closestDistance = DETECTION_RADIUS + 1
		
			for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if player ~= LocalPlayer and player.Character then
					local targetHRP = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					local targetHumanoid = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		
					if targetHRP and targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 then
						local offset = hrp.Position - targetHRP.Position
						local horizontalDistance = Vector3.new(offset.X, 0, offset.Z).Magnitude
						local heightDiff = math.abs(offset.Y)
		
						if horizontalDistance <= DETECTION_RADIUS and heightDiff <= DETECTION_HEIGHT and horizontalDistance < closestDistance then
							closestPlayer = player
							closestDistance = horizontalDistance
						end
					end
				end
			end
		
			return closestPlayer
		end
		
		-- Detection loop
		local function startDetection()
			if DetectionConnection then return end
		
			DetectionConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				if not Enabled then return end
		
				local character = LocalPlayer.Character
				if not character then return end
		
				local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if not hrp or not DetectionPart then return end
		
				local targetPlayer = findClosestTarget()
		
				if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
					local targetHRP = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		
					if targetHRP then
						CurrentTarget = targetPlayer
						faceTarget(targetHRP.Position)
						activateBat()
					end
				else
					CurrentTarget = nil
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- Function to stop detection
		local function stopDetection()
			if DetectionConnection then
				DetectionConnection:Disconnect()
				DetectionConnection = nil
			end
		
			if DetectionPart then
				DetectionPart:Destroy()
				DetectionPart = nil
			end
		
			CurrentTarget = nil
			isActivating = false
		end
		local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
			TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
		end
		-- Toggle button
		TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Enabled = not Enabled
		
			if Enabled then
				Tween(TextButton.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
		
				if LocalPlayer.Character then
					createDetectionCylinder()
				end
		
				LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
					if Enabled then
						task.wait(1)
						createDetectionCylinder()
					end
				end)
		
				startDetection()
			else
				Tween(TextButton.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
				stopDetection()
			end
		end)
		
		-- Cleanup on script destruction
		script.Destroying:Connect(function()
			stopDetection()
		end)
	end
	local function MCNFK_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.Frame.WalkToPlayerFrame.SwitchButton.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton2"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local PathfindingService = game:GetService("PathfindingService")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")
		local player = Players.LocalPlayer
		local button = script.Parent
		local isRunning = false 
		local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		
		local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
			TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
		end
		local function getOtherPlayer()
			local closestChar = nil
			local shortestDist = math.huge
			for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					local dist = (p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
					if dist < shortestDist then
						shortestDist = dist
						closestChar = p.Character
					end
				end
			end
			return closestChar
		end
		
		local function walkToTarget(humanoid, targetPosition)
			-- Create path
			local path = PathfindingService:CreatePath({
				AgentRadius = 2,
				AgentHeight = 5,
				AgentCanJump = true,
				WaypointSpacing = 4
			})
		
			local success, errorMessage = pcall(function()
				path:ComputeAsync(humanoid.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.Position, targetPosition)
			end)
		
			if not success or path.Status ~= Enum.PathStatus.Success then
				-- Fallback to direct movement if pathfinding fails
				humanoid:MoveTo(targetPosition)
				return
			end
		
			local waypoints = path:GetWaypoints()
		
			-- Handle waypoint reached
			local waypointConnection
			waypointConnection = humanoid.MoveToFinished:Connect(function(reached)
				if not isRunning then
					if waypointConnection then waypointConnection:Disconnect() end
					return
				end
			end)
		
			-- Move through waypoints
			for i, waypoint in ipairs(waypoints) do
				if not isRunning then
					if waypointConnection then waypointConnection:Disconnect() end
					return
				end
		
				humanoid:MoveTo(waypoint.Position)
		
				-- Handle jump waypoints
				if waypoint.Action == Enum.PathWaypointAction.Jump then
					humanoid.Jump = true
				end
		
				-- Wait for move to complete or timeout
				local timeout = 0
				while (humanoid.Parent.HumanoidRootPart.Position - waypoint.Position).Magnitude > 3 and timeout < 2 do
					task.wait(0.1)
					timeout = timeout + 0.1
					if not isRunning then break end
				end
			end
		
			if waypointConnection then waypointConnection:Disconnect() end
		end
		
		local function performAttack()
			if isRunning then return end 
		
			-- Character validation
			local character = player.Character
			if not character then 
				warn("No character found")
				return 
			end
		
			local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
			local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		
			if not (humanoid and rootPart) then 
				warn("Missing Humanoid or HumanoidRootPart")
				return 
			end
		
			local target = getOtherPlayer()
			if not target then 
				warn("No target found")
				return 
			end
		
			isRunning = true
		
			-- UI Update
			Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
				Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
			})
		
			-- Equip bat
			local bat = player.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Bat") or character:FindFirstChild("Bat")
			if bat and bat.Parent == player.Backpack then
				humanoid:EquipTool(bat)
				task.wait(0.15) -- Give time for equip
			end
		
			-- Movement loop with RunService for continuous updates
			local moveConnection
			local attackConnection
			local lastPathUpdate = 0
			local pathUpdateInterval = 0.5 -- Recompute path every 0.5 seconds
			local lastAttack = 0
			local ATTACK_COOLDOWN = 0.5
		
			local function cleanup()
				isRunning = false
				if moveConnection then
					moveConnection:Disconnect()
					moveConnection = nil
				end
			end
		
			moveConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				if not isRunning then
					cleanup()
					return
				end
		
				-- Refresh references
				if not (target and target.Parent and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
					warn("Target lost")
					cleanup()
					return
				end
		
				if not (character.Parent and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
					warn("Character lost")
					cleanup()
					return
				end
		
				local targetRoot = target.HumanoidRootPart
				local myRoot = character.HumanoidRootPart
				local distance = (targetRoot.Position - myRoot.Position).Magnitude
		
				-- Smoothly face the target using AlignOrientation or just MoveTo direction
				-- instead of forcing CFrame directly (which fights the physics engine)
				local lookPos = Vector3.new(targetRoot.Position.X, myRoot.Position.Y, targetRoot.Position.Z)
				if (lookPos - myRoot.Position).Magnitude > 0.01 then
					humanoid:MoveTo(myRoot.Position) -- keep position, let physics settle
					myRoot.CFrame = myRoot.CFrame:Lerp(CFrame.lookAt(myRoot.Position, lookPos), 0.15)
				end
		
				if distance > 4 then
					-- Update path periodically
					local currentTime = os.clock()
					if currentTime - lastPathUpdate > pathUpdateInterval then
						walkToTarget(humanoid, targetRoot.Position)
						lastPathUpdate = currentTime
					end
				else
					-- Close enough - attack with cooldown!
					local now = os.clock()
					if now - lastAttack >= ATTACK_COOLDOWN then
						bat = character:FindFirstChild("Bat")
						if bat then
							bat:Activate()
							lastAttack = now
						end
					end
				end
			end)
			-- Auto-stop after 30 seconds to prevent infinite running
			task.delay(30, function()
				if isRunning then
					isRunning = false
					if moveConnection then moveConnection:Disconnect() end
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- Stop function
		local function stopAttack()
			isRunning = false
			Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
				Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
			})
		
			-- Stop character movement
			if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				player.Character.Humanoid:MoveTo(player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
			end
		end
		
		-- Toggle behavior: click to start, click again to stop
		button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if isRunning then
				stopAttack()
			else
				performAttack()
			end
		end)
		
		UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
			if gameProcessed then return end 
			if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
				if isRunning then
					stopAttack()
				else
					performAttack()
				end
			end
		end)
	end
	local function KBEO_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.Frame.SlowModeFrame.SwitchButton.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton3"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

			TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
		end
		local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
		
		local SlowFallForce = nil
		local SlowFallAttachment = nil
		local SlowFallEnabled = false
		
		local function applySlowFall(enabled)
			SlowFallEnabled = enabled
		
			if enabled then
				if SlowFallForce then SlowFallForce:Destroy() SlowFallForce = nil end
				if SlowFallAttachment then SlowFallAttachment:Destroy() SlowFallAttachment = nil end
		
				if not LocalPlayer.Character then LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait() end
				local char = LocalPlayer.Character
				local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if not root then return end
		
				SlowFallAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment", root)
				SlowFallForce = Instance.new("VectorForce", root)
				SlowFallForce.Attachment0 = SlowFallAttachment
				SlowFallForce.RelativeTo = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
				SlowFallForce.Enabled = true
		
				task.spawn(function()
					while SlowFallEnabled and SlowFallForce and SlowFallForce.Parent do
						if root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Y < -2 then
							local totalMass = 0
							for _, part in pairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
								if part:IsA("BasePart") then
									totalMass += part:GetMass()
								end
							end
		
							SlowFallForce.Force = Vector3.new(0, totalMass * workspace.Gravity * 0.92, 0)
						else
							SlowFallForce.Force = Vector3.zero
						end
		
						task.wait(0.05)
					end
				end)
			else
				if SlowFallForce then SlowFallForce:Destroy() SlowFallForce = nil end
				if SlowFallAttachment then SlowFallAttachment:Destroy() SlowFallAttachment = nil end
			end
		end
		
		-- 🔘 BUTTON TOGGLE
		script.Parent.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			local isOff = script.Parent.Frame.Position == UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
		
			if isOff then
				Tween(script.Parent.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
				applySlowFall(true)
			else
				Tween(script.Parent.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
				applySlowFall(false)
			end
		end)
		
	end

	Converted["_borderGrandient7"].Name = "borderGrandient"
	Converted["_borderGrandient7"].Parent = Converted["_lemon3"]
	
	Converted["_UIStroke9"].Thickness = 2
	Converted["_UIStroke9"].Parent = Converted["_lemon3"]
	
	-- Fake Module Scripts:
	
	local fake_module_scripts = {}
	
	
	-- Fake Local Scripts:
	
	local function HZDJJ_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.drag
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "drag"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_Frame"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		
		local gui = script.Parent
		local dragFrame = gui
		
		local dragging = false
		local dragStart = nil
		local startPos = nil
		
		local frame = gui:WaitForChild("Frame")
		local sliderFrame = frame:FindFirstChild("SliderFrame")
		
		-- check if mouse is inside a gui object (by bounds)
		local function isInside(guiObject, mousePos)
			local absPos = guiObject.AbsolutePosition
			local absSize = guiObject.AbsoluteSize
		
			return mousePos.X >= absPos.X
				and mousePos.X <= absPos.X + absSize.X
				and mousePos.Y >= absPos.Y
				and mousePos.Y <= absPos.Y + absSize.Y
		end
		
		-- check if we are hovering excluded areas
		local function isMouseOverExcluded(mousePos)
			-- check Frame and ALL descendants
			if isInside(frame, mousePos) then
				return true
			end
		
			-- extra safety for slider
			if sliderFrame and isInside(sliderFrame, mousePos) then
				return true
			end
		
			return false
		end
		
		dragFrame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
			if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
		
				if isMouseOverExcluded(input.Position) then
					return
				end
		
				dragging = true
				dragStart = input.Position
				startPos = dragFrame.Position
		
				input.Changed:Connect(function()
					if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
						dragging = false
					end
				end)
			end
		end)
		
		UIS.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
			if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
				local delta = input.Position - dragStart
				dragFrame.Position = UDim2.new(
					startPos.X.Scale,
					startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
					startPos.Y.Scale,
					startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
				)
			end
		end)
	end
	local function EBVRL_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.borderStrke.borderGrandient.swift
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "swift"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_borderGrandient"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		local uiGradient = script.Parent
		local tweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		
		local gradientTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
			2,
			Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
			Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
			-1,
			false,
			0
		)
		
		tweenService:Create(uiGradient, gradientTweenInfo, {Rotation = 360}):Play()
	end
	local function USJBVS_fake_script() -- Fake Script: StarterGui..Frame.Frame.LocalScript
	    local script = Instance.new("LocalScript")
	    script.Name = "LocalScript"
	    script.Parent = Converted["_Frame1"]
	    local req = require
	    local require = function(obj)
	        local fake = fake_module_scripts[obj]
	        if fake then
	            return fake()
	        end
	        return req(obj)
	    end
	
		
		local RunService   = game:GetService("RunService")
		local Players      = game:GetService("Players")
		local UIS          = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
		
		local player    = Players.LocalPlayer
		local mouse     = player:GetMouse()
		local frame     = script.Parent  -- Frame1
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- Character / Humanoid helpers (respawn-safe)
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local char, hum, root
		local function getChar()
			char = player.Character
			if not char then return false end
			hum  = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			return hum and root
		end
		getChar()
		player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(c)
			char  = c
			hum   = c:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
			root  = c:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			-- Reattach LinearVelocity attachments on respawn
			task.wait(0.1)
			setupLinearVelocity()
		end)
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- State
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local state = {
			Speed   = { enabled = false, value = 28,   min = 0,  max = 150 },
			Jump    = { enabled = false, value = 50,   min = 0,  max = 150 },
			Gravity = { enabled = false, value = 50,   min = 0,   max = 225 },
		}
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- LinearVelocity setup  (Speed + Jump bypass)
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local speedLV, jumpLV, lvAttach
		
		local function setupLinearVelocity()
			if not getChar() then return end
		
			-- Clean up old instances
			if lvAttach and lvAttach.Parent then lvAttach:Destroy() end
		
			lvAttach  = Instance.new("Attachment")
			lvAttach.Name = "BoosterAttach"
			lvAttach.Parent = root
		
			-- Speed — horizontal plane velocity
			speedLV = Instance.new("LinearVelocity")
			speedLV.Name             = "SpeedLV"
			speedLV.Attachment0      = lvAttach
			speedLV.VelocityConstraintMode = Enum.VelocityConstraintMode.Plane
			speedLV.PrimaryTangentAxis  = Vector3.new(1, 0, 0)
			speedLV.SecondaryTangentAxis = Vector3.new(0, 0, 1)
			speedLV.PlaneVelocity    = Vector2.new(0, 0)
			speedLV.MaxForce         = 1e6
			speedLV.RelativeTo       = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
			speedLV.Enabled          = false
			speedLV.Parent           = root
		
			-- Jump — vertical impulse via separate LV
			jumpLV = Instance.new("LinearVelocity")
			jumpLV.Name             = "JumpLV"
			jumpLV.Attachment0      = lvAttach
			jumpLV.VelocityConstraintMode = Enum.VelocityConstraintMode.Line
			jumpLV.LineDirection    = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
			jumpLV.LineVelocity     = 0
			jumpLV.MaxForce         = 0  -- disabled until jump
			jumpLV.RelativeTo       = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
			jumpLV.Enabled          = true
			jumpLV.Parent           = root
		
			-- Hook jump input to fire upward impulse
			hum.Jumping:Connect(function(isJumping)
				if isJumping and state.Jump.enabled then
					local power = state.Jump.value
					jumpLV.LineVelocity = power
					jumpLV.MaxForce     = 1e6
					task.delay(0.15, function()
						jumpLV.MaxForce = 0
						jumpLV.LineVelocity = 0
					end)
				end
			end)
		end
		setupLinearVelocity()
		
		-- Drive speed LV each heartbeat based on move direction
		-- If HRP is stuck (position delta near zero while trying to move),
		-- fall back to direct CFrame offsetting so the player can still walk.
		local lastRootPos    = Vector3.new()
		local stuckFrames    = 0
		local STUCK_THRESHOLD = 0.02   -- studs moved per frame to be considered "not stuck"
		local STUCK_FRAMES    = 3      -- frames in a row with no movement = stuck
		RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
			if not (state.Speed.enabled and speedLV and speedLV.Parent) then
				if speedLV then speedLV.Enabled = false end
				stuckFrames = 0
				return
			end
			if not getChar() then return end
		
			local moveDir = hum.MoveDirection
			local currentWalkSpeed = hum.WalkSpeed
		
			-- Determine target speed: 29.5 if in 20-21 range, otherwise follow slider
			local targetSpeed = (currentWalkSpeed >= 20 and currentWalkSpeed <= 21) 
				and 29.5 
				or state.Speed.value
		
			local isMoving = moveDir.Magnitude > 0.1
		
			if isMoving then
				local flat = Vector2.new(moveDir.X, moveDir.Z).Unit * targetSpeed
		
				local currentPos = root.Position
				local delta = (currentPos - lastRootPos) * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)
				lastRootPos = currentPos
		
				if delta.Magnitude < STUCK_THRESHOLD then
					stuckFrames = stuckFrames + 1
				else
					stuckFrames = 0
				end
		
				if stuckFrames >= STUCK_FRAMES then
					speedLV.Enabled = false
					local dir3 = Vector3.new(moveDir.X, 0, moveDir.Z).Unit
					root.CFrame = root.CFrame + dir3 * targetSpeed * dt
				else
					speedLV.Enabled = true
					speedLV.PlaneVelocity = flat
				end
			else
				-- Auto-Regen: Reset velocity when idle to prevent jitter
				stuckFrames = 0
				speedLV.PlaneVelocity = Vector2.new(0, 0)
				speedLV.Enabled = false 
				lastRootPos = root and root.Position or lastRootPos
			end
		end)
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- Gravity bypass via metatable rawset unlock
		-- Attempts setreadonly unlock first; falls back
		-- to direct assignment (works on most executors)
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local originalGravity = workspace.Gravity
		
		local function setGravity(value)
			-- Method 1: getrawmetatable + setreadonly (executor-level)
			local success = pcall(function()
				local mt = getrawmetatable(workspace)
				local old = setreadonly(mt, false)
				rawset(workspace, "Gravity", value)
				setreadonly(mt, old)
			end)
			if not success then
				-- Method 2: Direct assignment fallback (works if __newindex isn't locked)
				pcall(function()
					workspace.Gravity = value
				end)
			end
		end
		
		local gravityLoop
		local function startGravityLoop()
			if gravityLoop then gravityLoop:Disconnect() end
			gravityLoop = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				if not state.Gravity.enabled then
					gravityLoop:Disconnect()
					gravityLoop = nil
					setGravity(originalGravity)
					return
				end
				-- Re-apply every frame to fight any game-side resets
				setGravity(state.Gravity.value)
			end)
		end
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- Toggle visual helper
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local ON_COLOR  = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)
		local OFF_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(77, 78, 97)
		local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
		
		local function setToggleVisual(toggleBtn, on)
			TweenService:Create(toggleBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {
				BackgroundColor3 = on and ON_COLOR or OFF_COLOR
			}):Play()
			toggleBtn.Text = on and "ON" or "OFF"
			TweenService:Create(toggleBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {
				TextColor3 = on and Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255) or Color3.fromRGB(211,211,211)
			}):Play()
		end
		
		
		local function makeSlider(section, trackFrame, knob, counter, minVal, maxVal)
			local dragging = false
		
			local function updateFromPos(xScale)
				xScale = math.clamp(xScale, 0, 1)
				local value = math.floor(minVal + (maxVal - minVal) * xScale)
				state[section].value = value
				counter.Text = tostring(value)
				-- Move knob (keep it anchored at center X = xScale)
				knob.Position = UDim2.new(xScale, 0, 0.5, 0)
			end
		
			-- Set initial knob position from default value
			do
				local initScale = (state[section].value - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal)
				knob.Position = UDim2.new(initScale, 0, 0.5, 0)
			end
		
			knob.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
				if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
					or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
					dragging = true
				end
			end)
		
			UIS.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
				if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
					or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
					dragging = false
				end
			end)
		
			-- Also allow clicking anywhere on the track to jump the knob
			trackFrame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
				if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
					or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
					dragging = true
					local absPos  = trackFrame.AbsolutePosition
					local absSize = trackFrame.AbsoluteSize
					local relX    = (input.Position.X - absPos.X) / absSize.X
					updateFromPos(relX)
				end
			end)
		
			UIS.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
				if not dragging then return end
				if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement
					or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
					local absPos  = trackFrame.AbsolutePosition
					local absSize = trackFrame.AbsoluteSize
					local relX    = (input.Position.X - absPos.X) / absSize.X
					updateFromPos(relX)
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		-- Wire up each section
		-- ──────────────────────────────────────────────
		local function wireSection(sectionName, onEnable, onDisable)
			local sectionFrame  = frame:WaitForChild(sectionName)
			local toggleBtn     = sectionFrame:WaitForChild("toggle")
			local counterLabel  = sectionFrame:WaitForChild("counter")
			local trackFrame    = sectionFrame:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Frame")       -- dark bar
			local knob          = trackFrame and trackFrame:WaitForChild("SliderFrame")
		
			if trackFrame and knob then
				makeSlider(sectionName, trackFrame, knob, counterLabel,
					state[sectionName].min, state[sectionName].max)
			end
		
			toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				local s = state[sectionName]
				s.enabled = not s.enabled
				setToggleVisual(toggleBtn, s.enabled)
				if s.enabled then
					onEnable()
				else
					onDisable()
				end
			end)
		end
		
		-- Speed
		wireSection("Speed",
			function() -- on enable — nothing extra; Heartbeat loop already handles it
			end,
			function() -- on disable
				if speedLV then
					speedLV.Enabled = false
					speedLV.PlaneVelocity = Vector2.new(0, 0)
				end
			end
		)
		
		-- Jump
		wireSection("Jump",
			function() end,
			function() end  -- disabling just means the Jumping hook checks state
		)
		
		-- Gravity
		wireSection("Gravity",
			function()
				startGravityLoop()
			end,
			function()
				setGravity(originalGravity)
			end
		)
		
	end
	
	coroutine.wrap(HZDJJ_fake_script)()
	coroutine.wrap(EBVRL_fake_script)()
	coroutine.wrap(USJBVS_fake_script)()
	]=]
			loadstring(code)()
		else
			game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "Error",
				Description = "Already launched",
				Duration = 5
			})
		end
	end)
end;

	-- ─── State ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local semiTPEnabled   = false

	-- ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

	end
	
	-- ─── Reset / flags ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function ResetToWork()
		local flags = {
			{"GameNetPVHeaderRotationalVelocityZeroCutoffExponent","-5000"},
			{"LargeReplicatorWrite5","true"},{"LargeReplicatorEnabled9","true"},

	local function executeTP(sequence)
		local char = player.Character
		local root = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local hum  = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
		if root and hum and backpack then
			local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild("Flying Carpet")
			if carpet then hum:EquipTool(carpet) task.wait(0.1) end
			root.CFrame = sequence[1] task.wait(0.1)
			root.CFrame = sequence[2]
		end
	end
	
	-- ─── Animal scanner ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function scanSinglePlot(plot)
		if not plot or not plot:IsA("Model") or isMyBase(plot.Name) then return end
		local podiums = plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums")
		if not podiums then return end
		for _, podium in ipairs(podiums:GetChildren()) do
			if podium:IsA("Model") and podium:FindFirstChild("Base") then
				table.insert(allAnimalsCache,{
					plot = plot.Name, slot = podium.Name,
					worldPosition = podium:GetPivot().Position,
					uid = plot.Name.."_"..podium.Name,
				})
			end
		end
	end
	
	local function initializeScanner()
		task.wait(2)
		local plots = workspace:WaitForChild("Plots", 10)
		for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do scanSinglePlot(plot) end
		plots.ChildAdded:Connect(scanSinglePlot)
		task.spawn(function()
			while task.wait(5) do
				table.clear(allAnimalsCache)
				for _, plot in ipairs(plots:GetChildren()) do scanSinglePlot(plot) end
			end
		end)
	end
	
	local function findPrompt(animal)
		local cached = PromptMemoryCache[animal.uid]
		if cached and cached.Parent then return cached end
		local plot   = workspace.Plots:FindFirstChild(animal.plot)
		local podium = plot and plot.AnimalPodiums:FindFirstChild(animal.slot)
		local prompt = podium and podium.Base.Spawn.PromptAttachment:FindFirstChildOfClass("ProximityPrompt")
		if prompt then PromptMemoryCache[animal.uid] = prompt end
		return prompt
	end
	
	local function buildStealCallbacks(prompt)
		if InternalStealCache[prompt] then return end
		local data = {holdCallbacks={}, triggerCallbacks={}, ready=true}
		local ok1, conns1 = pcall(getconnections, prompt.PromptButtonHoldBegan)
		if ok1 then for _, c in ipairs(conns1) do table.insert(data.holdCallbacks, c.Function) end end
		local ok2, conns2 = pcall(getconnections, prompt.Triggered)
		if ok2 then for _, c in ipairs(conns2) do table.insert(data.triggerCallbacks, c.Function) end end
		InternalStealCache[prompt] = data
	end
	
	local function executeInternalStealAsync(prompt, animalData, sequence)
		local data = InternalStealCache[prompt]
		if not data or not data.ready or IsStealing then return end
		data.ready = false IsStealing = true StealProgress = 0 CurrentStealTarget = animalData
		local tpDone = false
		task.spawn(function()
			for _, fn in ipairs(data.holdCallbacks) do task.spawn(fn) end
			local startTime = tick()
			while tick() - startTime < 1.3 do
				StealProgress = (tick() - startTime) / 1.3
				if StealProgress >= 0.73 and not tpDone then
					tpDone = true
					local hrp = getHRP()
					if hrp then
						local char = player.Character
						local hum  = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
						local bp   = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
						if hum and bp then
							local carpet = bp:FindFirstChild("Flying Carpet")
							if carpet then hum:EquipTool(carpet) task.wait(0.1) end
						end
						hrp.CFrame = sequence[1] task.wait(0.1)
						hrp.CFrame = sequence[2] task.wait(0.2)
						local d1 = (hrp.Position - pos1).Magnitude
						local d2 = (hrp.Position - pos2).Magnitude
						hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(d1 < d2 and pos1 or pos2)
					end
				end
				task.wait()
			end
			StealProgress = 1
			for _, fn in ipairs(data.triggerCallbacks) do task.spawn(fn) end
			task.wait(0.2)
			data.ready = true IsStealing = false StealProgress = 0 CurrentStealTarget = nil
		end)
	end
	
	local function getNearestAnimal()
		local hrp = getHRP()
		if not hrp then return nil end
		local nearest, dist = nil, math.huge
		for _, animal in ipairs(allAnimalsCache) do
			local d = (hrp.Position - animal.worldPosition).Magnitude
			if d < dist and d <= AUTO_STEAL_PROX_RADIUS then dist = d nearest = animal end
		end
		return nearest
	end
	
	local function getNearestPlayer()
		local char = player.Character
		if not char or not char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then return nil end
		local nearest, distance = nil, math.huge
		for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				local mag = (char.HumanoidRootPart.Position - p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
				if mag < distance then distance = mag nearest = p end
			end
		end
		return nearest
	end
