	Converted["_lemon3"].Size = UDim2.new(0.698623061, 0, 0.964354336, 0)
	Converted["_lemon3"].Name = "lemon"
	Converted["_lemon3"].Parent = Converted["_SemiTPFrame"]
	Converted["_borderGrandient6"].Color = ColorSequence.new{
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 206, 10)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 133, 11))
	}
	Converted["_borderGrandient6"].Name = "borderGrandient"
	Converted["_borderGrandient6"].Parent = Converted["_lemon3"]
	Converted["_UIStroke6"].Thickness = 2
	Converted["_UIStroke6"].Parent = Converted["_lemon3"]
	
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Text = ""
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].TextSize = 14
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(65, 62, 80)
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].BorderSizePixel = 0
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Position = UDim2.new(0.825539172, 0, 0.518055201, 0)
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Size = UDim2.new(0.189999998, 0, 0.742999971, 0)
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Name = "SwitchButton"
	Converted["_SwitchButton2"].Parent = Converted["_SemiTPFrame"]
	Converted["_UICorner8"].Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton2"]
	Converted["_borderStrke3"].ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
	Converted["_borderStrke3"].Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	Converted["_borderStrke3"].Thickness = 3
	Converted["_borderStrke3"].Name = "borderStrke"
	Converted["_borderStrke3"].Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton2"]
	Converted["_borderGrandient7"].Color = ColorSequence.new{
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 192, 2)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 133, 26))
	}
	Converted["_borderGrandient7"].Name = "borderGrandient"
	Converted["_borderGrandient7"].Parent = Converted["_borderStrke3"]
	Converted["_Frame5"].AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	Converted["_Frame5"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(27, 26, 31)
	Converted["_Frame5"].BorderSizePixel = 0
	Converted["_Frame5"].Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
	Converted["_Frame5"].Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	Converted["_Frame5"].Parent = Converted["_SwitchButton2"]
	Converted["_UIAspectRatioConstraint2"].Parent = Converted["_Frame5"]
	Converted["_UICorner9"].Parent = Converted["_Frame5"]
	
	-- ─── Progress Slider ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local ProgressFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
	ProgressFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	ProgressFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	ProgressFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.887087584, 0, 0.12, 0)
	ProgressFrame.Name = "ProgressFrame"
	ProgressFrame.Parent = Converted["_Frame2"]
	
	local sliderTrack = Instance.new("Frame")
	sliderTrack.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0.5)
	sliderTrack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(52, 52, 65)
	sliderTrack.BorderSizePixel = 0
	sliderTrack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.75, 0)
	sliderTrack.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 6)
	sliderTrack.Parent = ProgressFrame
	Instance.new("UICorner", sliderTrack).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
	
	local sliderFill = Instance.new("Frame")
	sliderFill.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0, 0.5)
	sliderFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 170, 0)
	sliderFill.BorderSizePixel = 0
	sliderFill.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
	sliderFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
	sliderFill.Parent = sliderTrack
	Instance.new("UICorner", sliderFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
	local sliderFillGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	sliderFillGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new{
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 206, 10)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 133, 26))
	}
	sliderFillGradient.Parent = sliderFill
	
	local sliderThumb = Instance.new("Frame")
	sliderThumb.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
	sliderThumb.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	sliderThumb.BorderSizePixel = 0
	sliderThumb.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
	sliderThumb.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
	sliderThumb.ZIndex = 2
	sliderThumb.Parent = sliderTrack
	Instance.new("UICorner", sliderThumb).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
	local sliderThumbStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	sliderThumbStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 170, 0)
	sliderThumbStroke.Thickness = 2
	sliderThumbStroke.Parent = sliderThumb
	
	local sliderLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	sliderLabel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 1)
	sliderLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	sliderLabel.BorderSizePixel = 0
	sliderLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.65, 0)
	sliderLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.6, 0)
	sliderLabel.Font = Enum.Font.FredokaOne
	sliderLabel.Text = "0%"
	sliderLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	sliderLabel.TextScaled = true
	sliderLabel.TextWrapped = true
	sliderLabel.ZIndex = 2
	sliderLabel.Parent = ProgressFrame
	local sliderLabelStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	sliderLabelStroke.Thickness = 2
	sliderLabelStroke.Parent = sliderLabel
	local sliderLabelGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	sliderLabelGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new{
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 206, 10)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 133, 26))
	}
	sliderLabelGradient.Parent = sliderLabel
	
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local p = math.clamp(StealProgress, 0, 1)
			sliderFill.Size      = UDim2.new(p, 0, 1, 0)
			sliderThumb.Position = UDim2.new(p, 0, 0.5, 0)
			sliderLabel.Text     = math.floor(p * 100 + 0.5) .. "%"
			task.wait(0.02)
		end
	end)
	
	-- ─── Toggle helper: no color change, dot slides X 0.25 ↔ 0.75, QuadOut ──────
	local function makeToggle(switchBtn, dotFrame, onToggle)
		local active = false
		local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
		switchBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			active = not active
			TweenService:Create(dotFrame, tweenInfo, {
				Position = active
					and UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
					or  UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
			}):Play()
			onToggle(active)
		end)
	end
	
	makeToggle(Converted["_SwitchButton"],  Converted["_Frame3"], function(state) _G.AutoPotion = state end)
	makeToggle(Converted["_SwitchButton1"], Converted["_Frame4"], function(state)
		speedAfterSteal = state
	end)
	makeToggle(Converted["_SwitchButton2"], Converted["_Frame5"], function(state) semiTPEnabled = state end)
	
	-- ─── Button callbacks ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	-- Activate (Reset)
	Converted["_button"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		local btn = Converted["_button"]
		btn.Active = false
		btn.Text = "Activating.."
		btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 56, 72)
		ResetToWork()
		task.delay(5, function()
			btn.Text = "Activated!"
		end)
	end)
	
	local function doBase2()
		if IsStealing then return end
		local animal = getNearestAnimal()
		if animal then
			local prompt = findPrompt(animal)
			if prompt then
				buildStealCallbacks(prompt)
				executeInternalStealAsync(prompt, animal, spot1_sequence)
			end
		end
	end
	
	local function doBase1()
		if IsStealing then return end
		local animal = getNearestAnimal()
		if animal then
			local prompt = findPrompt(animal)
			if prompt then
				buildStealCallbacks(prompt)
				executeInternalStealAsync(prompt, animal, spot2_sequence)
			end
		end
	end
	
	-- Base 2 (X)
	Converted["_button1"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(doBase2)
	
	-- Base 1 (C)
	Converted["_button2"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(doBase1)
	
	-- ─── Keyboard binds (X = Base 2, C = Base 1) ─────────────────────────────────
	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gpe)
		if gpe then return end
		if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.X then
			doBase2()
		elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.C then
			doBase1()
		end
	end)
	
	-- ─── Drag ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local gui = Converted["_Frame"]
	local dragging, dragStart, startPos
	
	gui.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos  = gui.Position
			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then dragging = false end
			end)
		end
	end)
	
	gui.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement and dragging then
			local delta = input.Position - dragStart
			gui.Position = UDim2.new(
				startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
				startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
			)
		end
	end)
	
	-- ─── Gradient rotation animation ─────────────────────────────────────────────
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			for i = 0, 360, 2 do
				Converted["_borderGrandient"].Rotation = i
				task.wait(0.01)
			end
		end
	end)
	
	-- ─── Proximity prompt hooks (Semi TP) ────────────────────────────────────────
	local currentEquipTask = nil
	local isHolding = false
	
	ProximityPromptService.PromptButtonHoldBegan:Connect(function(prompt, plr)
		if plr ~= player or not semiTPEnabled then return end
		isHolding = true
		if currentEquipTask then task.cancel(currentEquipTask) end
		currentEquipTask = task.spawn(function()
			task.wait(1)
			if isHolding and semiTPEnabled then
				local backpack = player:WaitForChild("Backpack", 2)
				if backpack then
					local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild("Flying Carpet")
					if carpet and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						player.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(carpet)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end)
	
	ProximityPromptService.PromptButtonHoldEnded:Connect(function(prompt, plr)
		if plr ~= player then return end
		isHolding = false
		if currentEquipTask then task.cancel(currentEquipTask) end
	end)
	
	ProximityPromptService.PromptTriggered:Connect(function(prompt, plr)
		if plr ~= player or not semiTPEnabled then return end
		local root = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if root then
			local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
			local hum = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			if backpack and hum then
				local carpet = backpack:FindFirstChild("Flying Carpet")
				if carpet then hum:EquipTool(carpet) task.wait(0.1) end
			end
			local d1 = (root.Position - pos1).Magnitude
			local d2 = (root.Position - pos2).Magnitude
			root.CFrame = CFrame.new(d1 < d2 and pos1 or pos2)
	
			if _G.AutoPotion then
				local bp = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
				if bp then
					local potion = bp:FindFirstChild("Giant Potion")
					if potion and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						player.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(potion)
						task.wait(0.1)
						pcall(function() potion:Activate() end)
					end
				end
			end
		end
		isHolding = false
	end)
	
	-- ─── Boot ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	-- Persistent speed boost: runs always, only applies when toggle is on + WalkSpeed 20-21
	RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not speedAfterSteal then return end
		local char = player.Character
		if not char then return end
		local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if not root or not humanoid then return end
		if humanoid.WalkSpeed < 20 or humanoid.WalkSpeed > 21 then return end
		if humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude == 0 then return end
		local moveDir = humanoid.MoveDirection.Unit
		root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(
			moveDir.X * 29.1,
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Y,
			moveDir.Z * 29.1
		)
	end)
	
	initializeScanner()
	]=]
			loadstring(code)()
		else
			game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
				Title = "Error",
				Description = "Already launched",
				Duration = 5
			})
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_c5);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.EspFrame.11.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_d4()
	local script = G2L["d4"];
	-- ESP PLAYER (BOX)
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Draws a 3D box hitbox around each player scaled to their character size,
	-- updates every RenderStepped. Optimized: reuses parts, only rebuilds on size change.

	local Players          = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService       = game:GetService("RunService")
	local TweenService     = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button      = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton     = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false

	-- BOX SETTINGS
	local BOX_COLOR      = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
	local BOX_THICKNESS  = 0.06   -- stud thickness of each edge part
	local BOX_TRANSPARENCY = 0    -- 0 = fully visible, 1 = invisible
	local NAME_TAG_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	-- ── BOX BUILDER ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	-- A box has 12 edges: 4 along X, 4 along Y, 4 along Z.
	-- We represent the box as a container Model with 12 thin Part "edges" + a BillboardGui name tag.

	local espContainers = {}  -- [Player] = { model, edges, billboard, lastSize }

	local function makeEdgePart(parent)
		local p = Instance.new("Part")
		p.Anchored    = true
		p.CanCollide  = false
		p.CanTouch    = false
		p.CanQuery    = false
		p.CastShadow  = false
		p.Material    = Enum.Material.Neon
		p.Color       = BOX_COLOR
		p.Transparency = BOX_TRANSPARENCY
		p.Size        = Vector3.new(BOX_THICKNESS, BOX_THICKNESS, BOX_THICKNESS)
		p.Parent      = parent
		return p
	end

	local function makeNameTag(adornee, name)
		local bb = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
		bb.AlwaysOnTop   = true
		bb.Size          = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 20)
		bb.StudsOffset   = Vector3.new(0, 3.5, 0)
		bb.MaxDistance   = 200
		bb.Adornee       = adornee
		bb.Parent        = adornee
		local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel", bb)
		lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		lbl.Size       = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
		lbl.Text       = name
		lbl.TextColor3 = NAME_TAG_COLOR
		lbl.Font       = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		lbl.TextSize   = 13
		lbl.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
		return bb
	end

	-- Returns the axis-aligned bounding box (CFrame center + Vector3 size)
	-- that fits around all visible BaseParts of a character.
	local function getCharBBox(char)
		local min, max = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge),
		Vector3.new(-math.huge, -math.huge, -math.huge)
		local found = false
		for _, part in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
			if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" and part.Transparency < 0.99 then
				local cf = part.CFrame
				local s  = part.Size * 0.5
				-- All 8 corners of this part
				for _, corner in ipairs({
					cf * CFrame.new( s.X,  s.Y,  s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new(-s.X,  s.Y,  s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new( s.X, -s.Y,  s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new(-s.X, -s.Y,  s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new( s.X,  s.Y, -s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new(-s.X,  s.Y, -s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new( s.X, -s.Y, -s.Z),
					cf * CFrame.new(-s.X, -s.Y, -s.Z),
					}) do
					local p = corner.Position
					min = Vector3.new(math.min(min.X, p.X), math.min(min.Y, p.Y), math.min(min.Z, p.Z))
					max = Vector3.new(math.max(max.X, p.X), math.max(max.Y, p.Y), math.max(max.Z, p.Z))
				end
				found = true
			end
		end
		if not found then return nil, nil end
		local center = (min + max) * 0.5
		local size   = max - min
		return CFrame.new(center), size
	end

	-- Position 12 edge parts to form a wireframe box at (cf, size).
	-- Edges array order: 4 top, 4 bottom, 4 verticals.
	local function positionEdges(edges, cf, size)
		local x, y, z = size.X * 0.5, size.Y * 0.5, size.Z * 0.5
		local t = BOX_THICKNESS

		-- Top 4 horizontal edges
		edges[1].Size  = Vector3.new(size.X, t, t)
		edges[1].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,  y,  z)
		edges[2].Size  = Vector3.new(size.X, t, t)
		edges[2].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,  y, -z)
		edges[3].Size  = Vector3.new(t, t, size.Z)
		edges[3].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new( x,  y, 0)
		edges[4].Size  = Vector3.new(t, t, size.Z)
		edges[4].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(-x,  y, 0)

		-- Bottom 4 horizontal edges
		edges[5].Size  = Vector3.new(size.X, t, t)
		edges[5].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0, -y,  z)
		edges[6].Size  = Vector3.new(size.X, t, t)
		edges[6].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0, -y, -z)
		edges[7].Size  = Vector3.new(t, t, size.Z)
		edges[7].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new( x, -y, 0)
		edges[8].Size  = Vector3.new(t, t, size.Z)
		edges[8].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(-x, -y, 0)

		-- 4 vertical edges
		edges[9].Size  = Vector3.new(t, size.Y, t)
		edges[9].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new( x, 0,  z)
		edges[10].Size = Vector3.new(t, size.Y, t)
		edges[10].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(-x, 0,  z)
		edges[11].Size = Vector3.new(t, size.Y, t)
		edges[11].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new( x, 0, -z)
		edges[12].Size = Vector3.new(t, size.Y, t)
		edges[12].CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(-x, 0, -z)
	end

	local function createESPForPlayer(plr)
		if espContainers[plr] then return end
		local model = Instance.new("Model")
		model.Name  = "ESP_" .. plr.Name
		model.Parent = workspace

		local edges = {}
		for i = 1, 12 do
			edges[i] = makeEdgePart(model)
		end

		espContainers[plr] = {
			model     = model,
			edges     = edges,
			billboard = nil,
			lastChar  = nil,
		}
	end

	local function removeESPForPlayer(plr)
		local entry = espContainers[plr]
		if not entry then return end
		if entry.model and entry.model.Parent then entry.model:Destroy() end
		espContainers[plr] = nil
	end

	local function cleanupAllESP()
		for plr, _ in pairs(espContainers) do
			removeESPForPlayer(plr)
		end
		espContainers = {}
	end

	-- ── RENDER LOOP ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local renderConn = nil

	local function startRender()
		if renderConn then return end
		renderConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if plr == LocalPlayer then continue end
				local entry = espContainers[plr]
				if not entry then continue end

				local char = plr.Character
				if not char then
					-- Hide edges
					for _, e in ipairs(entry.edges) do e.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -9999, 0) end
					continue
				end

				-- Rebuild name tag if character changed
				if entry.lastChar ~= char then
					if entry.billboard and entry.billboard.Parent then entry.billboard:Destroy() end
					local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					if hrp then
						entry.billboard = makeNameTag(hrp, plr.Name)
					end
					entry.lastChar = char
				end

				local cf, size = getCharBBox(char)
				if cf and size then
					positionEdges(entry.edges, cf, size)
				else
					for _, e in ipairs(entry.edges) do e.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -9999, 0) end
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	local function stopRender()
		if renderConn then renderConn:Disconnect(); renderConn = nil end
	end

	-- ── TOGGLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if plr ~= LocalPlayer then createESPForPlayer(plr) end
			end
			Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(plr)
				if plr ~= LocalPlayer and isEnabled then createESPForPlayer(plr) end
			end)
			Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(plr)
				removeESPForPlayer(plr)
			end)
			startRender()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			stopRender()
			cleanupAllESP()
		end
	end

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then toggle() end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_d4);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.Frame.EspFrame.12.SwitchButton.LocalScript
local function C_e5()
	local script = G2L["e5"];
	-- ESP BRAINROT
	-- script.Parent = TextButton
	-- Source: document 14 (leaked ESP script)
	-- Shows highest-gen animal billboard, timer on multiplier, player highlights

	local Players    = game:GetService("Players")
	local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local Workspace  = game:GetService("Workspace")

	local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
	local button      = script.Parent

	-- BINDING SYSTEM
	local bindButton     = script.Parent.Parent:WaitForChild("BindButton")
	local currentKeybind = nil
	task.spawn(function()
		while true do
			local bindText = bindButton.Text
			if bindText == "..." then currentKeybind = nil
			else
				local ok, kc = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[bindText] end)
				currentKeybind = (ok and kc) or nil
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
		end
	end)

	local isEnabled = false

	local function Tween(obj, time, style, direction, props)
		TweenService:Create(obj, TweenInfo.new(time, style, direction), props):Play()
	end

	-- ── SOURCE LOGIC ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
	local displayAssetId = 116155168863313
	local timerAssetId   = 128607699299345

	local DisplayTemplate, TimerTemplate

	local function safeLoadAsset(assetId)
		local ok, obj = pcall(function()
			return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. assetId)[1]
		end)
		return (ok and obj) or nil
	end

	-- Money parser from source
	local suffixes = { K=1e3, M=1e6, B=1e9, T=1e12, Qa=1e15, Qi=1e18 }
	local function parseGeneration(text)
		if not text then return 0 end
		text = text:match("^%$(.+)") or text
		text = text:gsub("/S$",""):gsub(",","")
		local numberStr = text:match("^[%d%.]+")
		local suffix    = text:match("[%a]+")
		local number    = tonumber(numberStr) or 0
		if suffix and suffixes[suffix] then number = number * suffixes[suffix] end
		return number
	end

	local function stripPossessive(s)
		if not s then return nil end
		s = s:gsub("%s+$",""):gsub("['']s$","")
		return s:gsub("%s+$","")
	end

	local function ieq(a,b)
		if not a or not b then return false end
		return string.lower(a) == string.lower(b)
	end

	local function anchorAllBaseParts(root)
		for _, d in ipairs(root:GetDescendants()) do
			if d:IsA("BasePart") then d.Anchored = true; d.CanCollide = false end
		end
	end

	-- State
	local currentHighestOverhead = nil
	local currentBillboard       = nil
	local currentModelHighlight  = nil
	local currentPartHighlight   = nil
	local currentMaxVal          = -1
	local currentTopOwnerName    = nil
	local plotToTimer            = {}
	local playerHighlights       = {}
	local espRenderConn          = nil
	local timerThread            = nil
	local playerESPConns         = {}
	local highestUpdateThread    = nil

	local function clearCurrentVisuals()
		if currentBillboard      then currentBillboard:Destroy();      currentBillboard = nil end
		if currentModelHighlight then currentModelHighlight:Destroy(); currentModelHighlight = nil end
		if currentPartHighlight  then currentPartHighlight:Destroy();  currentPartHighlight = nil end
	end

	local function resetCurrentHighest(setMaxToZero)
		clearCurrentVisuals()
		currentHighestOverhead = nil
		currentTopOwnerName    = nil
		currentMaxVal          = setMaxToZero and 0 or -1
	end

	local function getOwnerFromPlot(plot)
		local multiplierPart = plot:FindFirstChild("Multiplier", true)
		local parentForSign  = multiplierPart and multiplierPart.Parent or plot
		local plotSign = parentForSign:FindFirstChild("PlotSign") or parentForSign:FindFirstChild("PlotSign", true)
		if not plotSign then plotSign = plot:FindFirstChild("PlotSign", true) end
		if not plotSign then return nil end
		local label = plotSign:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TextLabel", true)
		return label and stripPossessive(label.Text) or nil
	end

	local function updateHighestDisplay()
		local plotsFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
		if not plotsFolder then return end
		resetCurrentHighest(true)
		local bestVal, bestOverhead, bestPlot, bestOwnerName = -1, nil, nil, nil
		for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
			if plot:IsA("Model") or plot:IsA("Folder") then
				local plotBestVal, plotBestOverhead = -1, nil
				for _, obj in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
					if obj.Name == "AnimalOverhead" and obj:IsA("BillboardGui") then
						local genLabel = obj:FindFirstChild("Generation")
						if genLabel and genLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
							local val = parseGeneration(genLabel.Text)
							if val > plotBestVal then plotBestVal = val; plotBestOverhead = obj end
						end
					end
				end
				if plotBestOverhead and plotBestVal > bestVal then
					local ownerName = getOwnerFromPlot(plot)
					if ownerName and not ieq(ownerName, LocalPlayer.Name) then
						bestVal = plotBestVal; bestOverhead = plotBestOverhead
						bestPlot = plot; bestOwnerName = ownerName
					end
				end
			end
		end
		if not bestOverhead then return end
		currentTopOwnerName = bestOwnerName
		currentHighestOverhead = bestOverhead; currentMaxVal = bestVal
		local originalDisplayName = bestOverhead:FindFirstChild("DisplayName")
		if not originalDisplayName then return end
		local baseParent = bestOverhead.Parent
		for _=1,4 do if baseParent then baseParent = baseParent.Parent end end
		local nameToFind, foundTargetChild = originalDisplayName.Text, nil
		for extra = 0, 2 do
			local candidate = baseParent
			for _=1, extra do if candidate then candidate = candidate.Parent end end
			if candidate then
				local child = candidate:FindFirstChild(nameToFind)
				if child then foundTargetChild = child; break end
			end
		end
		if not foundTargetChild then return end
		local modelHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
		modelHighlight.Adornee = foundTargetChild
		modelHighlight.FillTransparency = 0.75; modelHighlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)
		modelHighlight.OutlineTransparency = 0; modelHighlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)
		modelHighlight.Parent = foundTargetChild
		currentModelHighlight = modelHighlight
		local billboardParentPart = foundTargetChild:IsA("BasePart") and foundTargetChild
			or foundTargetChild:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
		if not billboardParentPart then return end
		if DisplayTemplate then
			local displayBillboard = DisplayTemplate:FindFirstChild("BillboardGui", true)
			if displayBillboard then
				local clone = displayBillboard:Clone()
				clone.AlwaysOnTop = true; clone.MaxDistance = 0
				clone.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,3,0)
				clone.Parent = billboardParentPart
				local cloneDisplay = clone:FindFirstChild("DisplayName", true)
				if cloneDisplay then cloneDisplay.Text = originalDisplayName.Text end
				local origGen  = bestOverhead:FindFirstChild("Generation")
				local cloneGen = clone:FindFirstChild("Generation", true)
				if cloneGen and origGen then cloneGen.Text = origGen.Text end
				currentBillboard = clone
			end
		end
		local partHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
		partHighlight.Adornee = billboardParentPart
		partHighlight.FillTransparency = 0.75; partHighlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)
		partHighlight.OutlineTransparency = 0;  partHighlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255,0,0)
		partHighlight.Parent = Workspace
		currentPartHighlight = partHighlight
	end

	local function startTimerLoop()
		if timerThread then return end
		timerThread = task.spawn(function()
			local plotsFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Plots")
			if not plotsFolder or not TimerTemplate then return end
			while isEnabled do
				for _, plot in ipairs(plotsFolder:GetChildren()) do
					if not plotToTimer[plot] then
						local multiplierPart = plot:FindFirstChild("Multiplier", true)
						if multiplierPart and multiplierPart:IsA("BasePart") then
							local timerClone = TimerTemplate:Clone()
							timerClone.Parent = plot
							anchorAllBaseParts(timerClone)
							if timerClone:IsA("Model") then
								if not timerClone.PrimaryPart then
									for _, d in ipairs(timerClone:GetDescendants()) do
										if d:IsA("BasePart") then timerClone.PrimaryPart = d; break end
									end
								end
								if timerClone.PrimaryPart then
									timerClone:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(multiplierPart.CFrame)
								end
							elseif timerClone:IsA("BasePart") then
								timerClone.CFrame = multiplierPart.CFrame
							else
								local anyBase = timerClone:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
								if anyBase then anyBase.CFrame = multiplierPart.CFrame end
							end
							local timerBillboard  = timerClone:FindFirstChild("BillboardGui", true)
							local timerTextLabel  = timerBillboard and timerBillboard:FindFirstChild("Timer", true)
							if timerBillboard and timerTextLabel and timerTextLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
								timerBillboard.AlwaysOnTop = true
								plotToTimer[plot] = { timerClone = timerClone, targetTextLabel = timerTextLabel }
							else
								timerClone:Destroy()
							end
						end
					end
					local entry = plotToTimer[plot]
					if entry and entry.targetTextLabel then
						local remainingTimeLabel
						for _, obj in ipairs(plot:GetDescendants()) do
							if obj.Name == "RemainingTime" and obj:IsA("TextLabel") then
								remainingTimeLabel = obj; break
							end
						end
						local sourceText = remainingTimeLabel and remainingTimeLabel.Text or ""
						if sourceText == "0" or ieq(sourceText,"0s") then
							entry.targetTextLabel.Text = "UNLOCKED"
							entry.targetTextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0)
						elseif sourceText == "" then
							entry.targetTextLabel.Text = "60s"
							entry.targetTextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
						else
							entry.targetTextLabel.Text = sourceText
							entry.targetTextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
						end
					end
				end
				task.wait(1)
			end
		end)
	end

	local function stopTimerLoop()
		timerThread = nil
		for plot, entry in pairs(plotToTimer) do
			if entry.timerClone then entry.timerClone:Destroy() end
			plotToTimer[plot] = nil
		end
	end

	local function addPlayerHighlight(plr)
		local function highlightChar(char)
			if playerHighlights[plr] then playerHighlights[plr]:Destroy() end
			local hl = Instance.new("Highlight")
			hl.Adornee = char
			hl.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(173,216,230)
			hl.FillTransparency = 0.75
			hl.OutlineTransparency = 0
			hl.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(173,216,230)
			hl.Parent = char
			playerHighlights[plr] = hl
		end
		if plr.Character then highlightChar(plr.Character) end
		local conn = plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char) highlightChar(char) end)
		table.insert(playerESPConns, conn)
	end

	local function forceCharacterVisible(char)
		for _, part in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
			if part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("Decal") then
				part.LocalTransparencyModifier = (part.Name == "HumanoidRootPart") and 1 or 0
			end
		end
	end

	local function enableESP()
		DisplayTemplate = safeLoadAsset(displayAssetId)
		TimerTemplate   = safeLoadAsset(timerAssetId)

		-- Player highlights + force-visible
		for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if plr ~= LocalPlayer then addPlayerHighlight(plr) end
		end
		local pAddConn = Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(plr)
			if plr ~= LocalPlayer then addPlayerHighlight(plr) end
		end)
		table.insert(playerESPConns, pAddConn)

		-- Force-visible render loop
		espRenderConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			if not isEnabled then return end
			for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if plr ~= LocalPlayer then
					local char = Workspace:FindFirstChild(plr.Name)
					if char then forceCharacterVisible(char) end
				end
			end
		end)

		-- Highest gen display loop
		updateHighestDisplay()
		highestUpdateThread = task.spawn(function()
			while isEnabled do updateHighestDisplay(); task.wait(2) end
		end)

		startTimerLoop()
	end

	local function disableESP()
		if espRenderConn    then espRenderConn:Disconnect();    espRenderConn = nil end
		highestUpdateThread = nil  -- stops the while loop

		-- Remove player highlights
		for plr, hl in pairs(playerHighlights) do
			if hl and hl.Parent then hl:Destroy() end
		end
		playerHighlights = {}
		for _, conn in ipairs(playerESPConns) do conn:Disconnect() end
		playerESPConns = {}

		clearCurrentVisuals()
		stopTimerLoop()
	end

	-- SHARED TOGGLE
	local function toggle()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled
		if isEnabled then
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.75, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			enableESP()
		else
			pcall(function()
				Tween(button.Frame, 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, {
					Position = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.5, 0)
				})
			end)
			disableESP()
		end
	end

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggle)

	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if gameProcessed then return end
		if currentKeybind and input.KeyCode == currentKeybind then toggle() end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_e5);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.TextButton.LocalScript
local function C_f4()
	local script = G2L["f4"];
	local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

	local button = script.Parent
	local arrow = button.TextLabel
	local frame = button.Parent.Frame

	local isEnabled = false

	-- where it sits normally
	local shownPosition = frame.Position

	-- slightly above for opening animation
	local hiddenUp = shownPosition - UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.15, 0)

	-- to the RIGHT for closing animation
	local hiddenRight = shownPosition + UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0, 0)

	-- start hidden
	frame.Position = hiddenUp
	frame.Visible = false

	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
		0.35,
		Enum.EasingStyle.Sine,
		Enum.EasingDirection.Out
	)

	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		isEnabled = not isEnabled

		-- arrow rotation
		local targetRotation = isEnabled and 180 or 0
		TweenService:Create(arrow, tweenInfo, {
			Rotation = targetRotation
		}):Play()

		if isEnabled then
			frame.Visible = true

			-- make sure it starts above before sliding down
			frame.Position = hiddenUp

			TweenService:Create(frame, tweenInfo, {
				Position = shownPosition
			}):Play()
		else
			-- slide RIGHT when closing
			local tween = TweenService:Create(frame, tweenInfo, {
				Position = hiddenRight
			})

			tween:Play()
			tween.Completed:Wait()

			frame.Visible = false

			-- reset back above so next open animation works
			frame.Position = hiddenUp
		end
	end)
	local gui = script.Parent -- this can be a Frame, TextButton, ImageButton, etc.

	local UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService")

	local dragging = false
	local dragStart = nil
	local startPos = nil

	-- start dragging when clicked
	gui.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = gui.Position

			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
					dragging = false
				end
			end)
		end
	end)

	-- detect mouse movement globally (works for TextButtons too)
	UIS.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
			local delta = input.Position - dragStart

			gui.Position = UDim2.new(
				startPos.X.Scale,
				startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
				startPos.Y.Scale,
				startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
			)
		end
	end)
end;
task.spawn(C_f4);
-- StarterGui.openLmn.TextButton.borderStrke.borderGrandient.swift
local function C_fa()
	local script = G2L["fa"];
	local uiGradient = script.Parent
	local tweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

	local gradientTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
		2,
		Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
		Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,
		-1,
		false,
		0
	)

	tweenService:Create(uiGradient, gradientTweenInfo, {Rotation = 360}):Play()
end;
task.spawn(C_fa);

return G2L["1"], require;
